common thraldome bothe city future fortune thei trie proue sone clashyng armure sounde firste incountrie glitteryng swordes shine incredible horror feare perced beholder hope inclining neither partes voice mindes whist silent thei closed together onely mouyng body doubtfull weldyng handlyng weapon blooddie woundes appered twoo romanes fallyng doune starke deade one vpon three albanes sore hurt whereat albane hoste shouted ioye romane legion voide hope amazed see one remain three chauced liued whiche one alone vnmeete matche rest euen fierce thought hymself good inough therefore separate fight fleeth backe meanyng thereby giue euery welcome thei followed whe retired good space place thei fought lookyng backe sawe followe good distance one one hard vpon let driue greate violence while albane hoste cried vpon curatij help brother horatius killed enemie demaunded seconde battaill romanes incoraged chapion acclamation shoutes fearfull men wont doe vpon sodaine spedeth hymself sight could ouertake hym whiche farre killed curatij thei equallie matched one one hope strengthe vnlike one free wounde hurte cruell fierce reason double victorie fainct losse bloodde wearie runnyng pantyng breath discomfited brethren slaughter slaine hym obiected fight victorious enemie whiche equall matche horatius reioysing saied twoo thy brother haue dispatched thirde cause battaill take hande romanes maie bee lordes albanes curiatius able sustaine blowe fill doune liyng vpon backe thruste hym throte sworde whiche dooen dispoiled hym armure romanes great triumphe reioyse interteigned horatius ioye greater feare ouerthrowe nerer combate beyng ended albanes became subiecte romanes metius departed asked tullus would co maunde hym seruice willed hym keepe young souldiours still interteignemente would require aide againste vere te armie dissolued horatius like conquerour marched home rome three spoiles enemy beyng borne hym saied horatius sister whiche espoused one curatij slaine meetyng brother triumphe one gate called capena knowyng coate armure paramour borne vpo brother shulders wrought made owne handes tore rente heare hedde moste pitiouslie bewailed death beloued brother beyng pride victorie taking lametacion sister disdainfull part drewe sworde thruste saiyng opprobrious woordes auaunte thy vnreasonable loue get thee thy spouse hast thou forgotten death thy twoo brother bee slaine prosperous successe thy victorious brother chieflie happie deliueraunce thy countrie let romane woman soeuer bee take like rewarde shall bewaile death enemie whiche horrible facte seemed moste cruell father people whiche offence brought king deliuered iudged accordyng lawe lawe condempned appealed people appeale p horatius father spake wordes doughter slain without iust desert whiche would haue sued condigne punishment executed vpo sone accordyng naturall pietie father wherfore beseche dooe suffer haue seen time past beautified noble race progenie child bee vtterly destitute voide together embrased sonne emonges shewed spoiles curatiens saiyng ca abide see noble champion ye romanes lately ye behelde goe order triumphe victorious maner lye bounde vnder gibet expecting tormetes death whiche cruell deformed sight albanes eye well able beholde goe thou hangman binde ha de hym hath atchieued romane people glorious empire goe saie couer face hath deliuered citie thraldome bo dage hang vpon vnhappy tree scourge hym place within citie either emonges triumphes spoiles enemy doe remaine el without walles emonges graues vanquished whether ye dauise carrie hym honourable worthie actes shall reuenge villanie cruell death people hearyng lamentable talke father seyng hym vnmoueable mynde able sustaine aduersitie acquited hym rather admiracion vertue valiance iustice equitie cause suche straicte order iustice emonges romanes although yong gentilman vindicated countrie seruitute bondage noble memorie perfecte manhode yet reason murdre committed vpon owne sister thei straict stacke grauntyng hym pardon thei would incorage posteritie like inconuenience prouoke well doer glorie triumphe perpetrate thynges vnlawfull sextus tarquinius rauisheth lucrece bewailyng losse chastitie killeth self pthe seconde nouell greate preparacion made romanes people called rutuli citie named ardea excellyng wealth richesse whiche cause romane kyng beyng exhausted quite voide money reason sumptuous buildynges made warres vpon countrie tyme siege citee yong romane gentleman baqueted one emonges one called collatinus tarquinius sonne egerius chaunce thei entred communicacion wiues euery one praisyng seuerall spouse length talke began growe hotte vpon collatinus said wordes wer vaine within fewe howers might tried muche wife lucrecia excell rest wherfore q liuelihod let v take horse proue whiche wiues doth furmout wherevpo thei rode rome poste coming thei found kynges doughters sportyng themselfes sundrie pastymes thence thei went house collatinus thei founde lucrece named spendyng time idlenes late night occupied busie emonges maides middes house spinning wolle victorie praise wherof giuen lucretia sawe husbande gently louingly interteigned hym curteously biddyng tarquinians welcome imediatlie sextus tarquinius sonne tarquinius superbus tyme romane kyng attached incensed libidious desire construprate defloure lucrece yong gentleman bestowed night pleasantlie wiues thei retourned campe long sextus tarquinius one man returned collatia vnknowen collatinus ignoraunte lucrece reste houshold purpose came beyng right hartely interteigued supper conueighed chamber tarquinius burnyng loue lucrece perceiued housholde bee reste thynges quiet naked sworde hande goeth lucrece beyng slepe kepyng doune lefte hande saied holde thy peace lucrece q sextus tarquinius sworde hande thou crie kill thee gentlewoman beyng sore fraied newlie awaked slepe seyng iminent death could tell doe tarquinius confessed loue began intreate therewithall vsed sundrie menacyng woordes meanes attemptyng make quiet sawe obstinate would yelde requeste notwithstandyng cruell threates added shamefull villanous woordes saiyng would kill slaine would also kill slaue place hym might reported slain beyng taken adulterie vaquished terrible infamous threat fleshly licencious enterprise ouercame puritie chast harte whiche doen departed lucrece made haste lucrece thei founde sittyng verie pensife sadde chamber sone sawe theim began pitiouslie weepe housebande asked whether thynges well vnto saied woordes dere housebande bee well safe vnto woman hath loste chastitie ala collatine steppe man fixed thy bedde bodie onely violated minde god knoweth gililes whereof death shalbe witnesse men giue ha de trouthe adulterer maie escape vnreuenged sextus tarquinius beyng enemie stede frende night came vnto armed sworde hand violence caried waie tooke pestiferous ioye euery gaue faith comforted pensife languishyng ladie imputing offence aucthor doer affirmyng bodie polluted mynde consente crime absent wherevnto added praie consider selues punishment due malefactour parte though clere self offence bodie shall feele punishemente vnchast ill theimselues presse readie attempt enterprise guarrison placed bestowed collatia diligente watche warde kepte gate citie intent kyng haue aduertismente slurre reste souldiours followed brutus rome whe huge armie whose wo derfully appail senate like occasion terrour neuer tyme chaunced romanes onely feare enemy also owne subiectes suspecting lest thei forced reteine kinges afterwardes wisedome guarrisons kepte walles waie ouer tybre whiche thought verie saufe defensible although wodde bridge made ouer riuer almoste open waie enemy entrie whereof horacius cocles fortune serued daie charge manfully behaued broken vp burned bridge dooen notable exploites defended passage suche valiance defence thereof seemed miraculous great astonishemet enemy fine porsenna seyng could little preuaile afsault retourned campe determynyng neuerthelesse continue siege whiche tyme one caius mutius yong gentleman rome purposed aduenture notable enterprise saiyng senator wordes determine passe riuer enter campe enemy fetche spoile reuege mutuall iniuries hazarde greater enterprise goddes assistaunt vnto senate vnderstandyng effect indeuour allowed deuise hauyng sworde vnder garmente went foorthe come throng conueighed hymself uere kynges pauilion could chaunced paiyng wage souldiours secretarie sitte suche apparell almoste kyng hymself weare mutius beyng ferde demaunde whiche theim kyng lest betraie hymself sodainly killed secretarie stede kyng makyng waie blouddie sworde escape apprehended brought kyng merueilous stoutnesse audacitie spake wordes citizen rome name mutius beyng enemie would faine haue killed myne enemie whiche attempte esteme die cared committe murder naturally giuen romanes bothe valiantly doe stootely suffer alone haue conspired thy death greate nomber v haue promised like hope aspire seblable praise glorie wherefore beginnyng doe please thee make thy self redie euery hower expecte like perill fight thy self make accompte euery daie euen doore thy lodgyng thy enemie armed doeth awaite thee alone yong gentleman citie dooe stande defiance pronounce vpon thee kinde battaill feare army hostilitie thee alone euery one v warres shalbe tried king astoned holde desperate enterprice fill greate rage furie commaundyng mutius presently bee consumed fire vnlesse would hande tel order purposed diuised treason beholde king q litell thei care body dooe aspire seeke fame glorie thrust right hande fire rosted flame like one wittes kyng amazed straungenesse facte stepped doune seate caused hym taken fire saiyng awaie frende q kyng thou hast killed thy self aduentured hostilitie vpo thy self rather surely would think self happie like valiance found countrie wherefore lawe armes sette thee libertie vntouched without harme wherevnto mutius acquilyng deserte answered muche thou hast thus honourably delte recompence benefite saie thus muche vnto thee threates thou shouldest neuer haue gotten hades three hundred v yong noble men rome haue conspired thy death euen like attempt lofte come first rest whe fortune shall giue oportunitie tyme euery one tourne giue aduenture wherevpon dismissed afterwardes called scaeuola losse right hande peace offered romanes vpon codicions enemy guarrisons withdrawen ianiculum countrie wonne veientines bee restored againe gaue hostage emonges gentlewoman called cloelia deliuered handes hetrurians deceiuyng would wishe whiche haue felte greate losse decaie cause securitie presente rather suffered patience desert bee instaunte greate multitude volscians game prepared citie throughly bent beholde dooe chaunced immediatly decree order pronou ced publius numitorius maides vncle mother side icilius beloued comen home vpon whose retourne incontinently icilius approched nere appius put backe sergeant cried loude woordes thou oughteste put backe hence appius sworde thou mightest without let enioye thyng thou wouldest haue kept close secrete dooe purpose marie maide doubt right honest chaste also pudique pure virgin wherfore call together thy secgeantes cause roddes are made prest redie assure thee spouse icilius shall remaine father house although thou hast taken awaie romane people tribune aide appeales whiche twoo stronge fortes holdes common libertie aucthoritie giuen thee libidinously abuse wiues childre excercise thy crueltie behind backes vpon liues thou liste thou dooe contaminate defile vertue chastitie wherevnto thou inferre damage iniurie myne owne part loue beloued crie aide romanes present virginius shall doe like souldiours quarrel owne doughter al together wil implore succour goddes menne truste thou shalt enioye thy purpose v haue lost liues wherefore appius aduise thee take heede time virginius doeth come seke remedie defende doughter knowe condicion sorte ordred bee referred seruitude man parte life shall soner faile defending libertie faithe betrouthed appius perceiuyng constancie icilius people greate mutine sturre differred cause virginia till nexte daie whose frendes hoped tyme father would home wherefore expedicion thei addressed messenger vnto hym campe saufgarde doughter consisted presence meane time assertor required maide offeryng put surety enemie father seyng voide succour helpe defende innocencie doughter spake appius sorte firste dooe beseche thee appius haue vsed vnreasonable woordes againste thee pardon impute father grief sorowe suffer praie thee examine nonrsse presence wench whole circumstance matter intent bee supposed father maie departe hence quiet conscience satisfied contented virginius hauyng license talke doughter noursse departed side place called cloacina shoppes called taberne nouae pluckyng sharpe knife bocher stoode thruste hart doughter saiyng meanes doughter make thee free loking towardes iudgement feate saied bloodde appius consecrate bestowe vpon thee whiche doen sworde made waie passe throng conueigh hymself citie icilius nnmitorius tooke vp deade bodie shewed people cried vpo wickednesse appius bewailyng vnhappie beautie faire maiden deplored necessitie father woman exclamed lamentable wise saiing condicion state bring foorthe child bee rewardes chastitie suche like pitifull cry woman wont astonied whole campe muche euery man demaunded cause sodain chaunce virginius could speake teares length disclosed vnto effecte whole matter holdyng vp handes towardes heauens saied beseche deare companion doe impute wickednesse appius claudius vpon ne yet parricide murderer myne owne childre life deare doughter acceptable myne owne life bee might haue continued free woman honest virgine sawe ledde rape like bondewoman considered better life lost suffered liue shame wherfore naturall pitie conuerted kinde crueltie mine owne part doe passe liue log thought haue helpe succour reuenge death consider selues haue doughters sister wiues think therefore fleshly desire appius satisfied death doughter longer dooeth continue securite vnbrid led appetite let calamitie sufficiet documet beware like iniuries wife deade naturall fate constellacion bicause doughter could continewe longer honeste chaste life death befallen vnto whiche although bee miserable yet honourable place house appius satisfie filthy luste faile purpose doe reuenge death doughter good vpon fleshe discharge dishonour seruitude violente crnell handes succlamacion pitifull complainte stirred multitude thei promised helpe relieue sorowe whervpon whole campe mutine marched order battaile moute auentine virginius perswaded souldiours chose ten principall capitaines bee heade chief enterprise whiche honourable title field called tribuni virginius hymself beyng elected chief tribune saied woordes souldiours praie reserue estimacion conceiue vntill better tyme apter occasion aswell commoditie self death doughter wil suffer honour pleasaunte welcome duryng life moreouer troubled state common wealthe meete gouernours subiecte occurant enuie reproche seruice shal profitable vnto whe haue thus created tribune shall lesse commodious doe still remaine priuate manne spoken woordes thei chose tenne tribune like campe mounte auentine prouoked stirred sedicio euen meanes icilius nomitorius remembred armie beyng sabine began reuolt made like nomber tribune whiche arraie battaile marched citee gate collina banner displaied ioyne cape vpo mount auentine bothe campes assembled thei twoo emonges twentie tribune bee generalles called oppius sextus manilius senate carefull pensife euentes eftsons assembled certaine determinacion agreed vpon length thei concluded valerius horatius sent mount auentine perswade furie anger ought rather bee pardoned permitted graunted ye beare face seeme detest hate seueritie ye selues incurre runne hedlong kinde crueltie ye made free selues ye desire lordes ouer aduersaries require viewe beholde ladie maistres sorte woman seen naked doeth clothes put also chastitie olde tyme honest thinges deuised mannes instruction emonges whiche vsed one thing euery man ought behold thinges owne sir doe beleue assuredlie fairest woman worlde wherfore desire thynges bee vnlawfull sorte gyges replied yet feared lest dau ger might happen vnto hym candaules encouraged saiyng good afraid either wife goe aboute deceiue thee thou shalte incurre daunger take vpon vse matter meanes shal knowe thou haste seen place thee behinde portall chamber goe bed wife commonlie dooeth followe beyng chamber chaire sette redie vpon whiche laieth clothes putteth doen sheweth self good tyme naked riseth chaire goe bedde backe beyng toward thee thou maiest easilie conueighe thy self againe anywise take heede doe see thee thou goest wherevnto praie thee haue speciall regarde gyges seeyng meanes could auoide vaine requeste kyng redie tyme appoincted candaules hower bedde tyme went chamber conueighed gyges kyng quene followed gyges behelde goyng puttyng clothes backe towardes hym goyng perceiued hym quene vnderstanding housbande circumstance facte neither shame crie ne yet made countenance though seen gyges minde purposed reuenge husbandes follie emoges lydia parte nacions coumpted greate shame see naked man gentlewoman counterfaited grief kepte silence mornyng redie suche seruauntes moste trusted sent gyges thought knowen nothyng whiche chauced many time vsed haue accesse quene called beyng come presence saied vnto gyges offer vnto thee two condicions take whether thou wilte either thou muste kill candaules take thy wife kyngdome also el thou must die thy self thou maiest vnderstande thynges meete knowen necessary obeie candaules either must needes die whiche gaue thee counsaile thy self whiche diddest see naked therby committed thyng vnlawfull whiche woordes wonderfully amase gyges beseched quene would pardon hym fro vnlawful choise sawe could perswade required shewe meanes might attempte enterprise marie q euen place thou sawest naked slepe thou shalte committe facte thei deuised treason nighte approched gyges stoute courage bente hymself therevnto home garden yonge lactuse beginne growe cutte bitter sower stalkes pitie mother lactuse sustaine sorowe bastarde degenerate shrubbes whiche beyng taken awaie prospereth encreaseth greate swetenesse persian called sinaetas farre owne house mette king artaxerxes wherewith present order emonges persian instituted lawe euery man whiche mette king giue hym present wherefore poore man bicause would neglecte duetie ranne riuer called cyrus taking vp bothe handes full water spake kyng wise beseche god maiestie maie euermore raigne emonges occasion place myne abilitie instant serueth come honour maiestie intente maie passe without presente whiche cause giue vnto water grace one incamped self would goe home house best derest thing haue honour maiestie withall peradueture shall muche inferiour giftes whiche dooe giue artaxerxes delighted chaunce saied vnto hym good followe thanke thee present assure thee acceptable vnto precious gift worlde first bicause water best thynges bicause riuer whiche thou diddest take dooeth beare name cyrus wherefore commaunde thee come campe spoken wordes required eunuch take present putte cuppe golde kyng lodged pauilion sente man persian robe cuppe golde thousande darices coigne emoges persian whervpon image darius willyng messenger saie vnto hym woordes hath pleased kyng thou shouldest delight thy self make merie golde thou diddest exhilarate minde suffryng hym passe without honour present necessitie serue thee diddeste humblie salute hym water pleasure also thou shalte drinke water cuppe golde whiche thou madest hym partaker artaxerxes hereby expressed true image princely mynde would disdaine cherefully beholde homelie gifte estimacion rude nothyng worthe handes poore subiecte liberally reward ductifull zeale thinges greate price reioysyng recompenced hym princely rewardes saiyng sone common othe persian kynges manne able suche trauell diligence iudgement make litle citie one shalbe large greate whiche wordes seme declare thynges care sufficiente paine continuall labour maie nature made excellent better loue chariton menalippes pthe x nouell rehearse facte tyrant phalaris farre discrepante condictons fauoureth greate kindnes humanitie seemeth bee dooen chariton agrigentine borne greate louer beautie ardente affection loued one menalippus whiche also borne citie honeste condicions excellent beautie tyrant phalaris hindred menalippus certaine sute contended iudgement one phalaris frendes tyraunte commaunded hym giue ouer suite wherevnto bicause obediente threatned put hym death except would yelde menalippus ouer came hym lawe noble men whiche wer frendes phalaris would giue sentence brought nonesuite whiche yong manne takyng ill parte saied receiued wronge confessed frende chariton wronge susteined requiryng aide reuenge vpon tirant made yong menne priuie conspiracie suche knewe would redie apt enterprise chariton perceiuyng rage furie frende knowyng man would take parte feare tyraunte began disswade hym saiyng hymself went like attempt litle deliuer countrie libertie presente seruitude able sorte purpose without greate daunger wherefore praied hym committe consideracion thereof vnto suffre hym espie tyme apt conuenient menalippus contente chariton reuoluyng hymself deuise would make dere frende partaker fact lest perceiued alone toke vpon hym doe deede onely hymself might susteine smarte wherefore takyng sworde hande sekyng waie giue assaulte vpon tiraunte enterprise disclosed chariton apprehended guarde whiche tirantes defence diligentlie attended hym thence sent iaole examined vpon interrogatory bewraie reste conspiratours whiche suffered racke violence tormetes afterwardes menalippus remembryng constancie frende crueltie stoutly suffered wente phalaris confessed vnto hym onely priuie treason also aucthour thereof phalaris demaundyng cause told hym consideracion rehersed whiche reuokyng sentence iniuries doen vnto tirant merueiling constante frendship twaine acquited bothe comelinesse although attired simple apparell teares manifestly ran doune eye falling vpon garmentes distillyng doune feete moste auncient emonges v saied good chere ladie haue verie valiant man housbande notwithstandyng wee haue chosen gentleman inferiour hym either beautie force wisedome valiance thinke bee man worlde worthie admiracion cyrus prince lorde whose paragon wee haue chosen bee ladie heard saie tare attiremente heade bodie cried maides skriched tyme greatest parte face appered necke handes assure self cyrus v whiche viewed well semed impossible suche creature could borne mortall parentes asia therfore sir looke vpon wise cyrus saied praise ye giue lesse mynde haue see suche one haue saied quod araspas bicause saied cyrus goe see hearyng make reporte beautie leasure seruyng therevnto fraied lest would sone allure goe many tymes beholde whereby might perchaunce growe negliget matter greatest importance yonge manne smilyng saied thinke cyrus beautie woman force man vnwillyng attempt thyng best nature haue force would compell men like doe see fire burneth men one sorte bicause nature beautifull thynges bee equall estimacion bee greate price dooe regarde loue voluntarie thyng euery manne loueth liste brother loue sister loued father loue doughter yet loued feare lawe sufficient refraine loue lawe made commaunde men thei whiche eate bee hungrie thei drinke thirst manne colde winter hotte sommer lawe could compell men obeye thynges menne nature bee subiecte vnto theim loue thyng free voluntarie euery man loueth thynges bee owne apparell necessary wherevnto cyrus replied loue bee voluntarie bee man maie abandon liste haue seen men wepe sorowe loue haue knowen haue slaues loue thei haue loued haue thought thraldome greatest euill giuyng awaie many thinges whiche better haue kepte haue praied god exonerated loue aboue disease yet could bee deliuered beeyng bounde stronger imprisonment thei tied chaines yeldyng themselues louers seruyng obedience thei hampered suche mischieues thei seeke auoide theim thei doe deede saie answered yonge man therefore suche louers miserable wherby thei wishe dye still continuyng woe calamitie thousand way ridde life yet thei die fall stealyng robbyng menne thei haue robbed firste thinkyng theft vnnecessarie doe condempne theues doe pardon punishe like maner beautifull doe counsell menne loue couet lawfull miserable men shewyng themselues inferiour lustes desire dooe ende accuse loue aucthour miserie good honest men although thei desire golde beautifull horsses faire woman yet thei abstaine subiecte meete self haue beholden woman whiche semeth bee surpassyng faire wight yet ride dooe thynges accordyng duetie paraduenture saied cyrus went soner awaie loue could haue time fasten vpon man fire touchyng man doeth straite burne woodde flame yet would willingly touche fire beholde beautifull persones would giue counsaill araspas beware suffer eye rolle wander vpon faire woman fire burneth touche beautifull folke doe kindle beholde farre suche wise thei burne loue warraunte cyrus saied araspas dooe continually looke vpon drowned loue shall prouoke thing doeth become saie well saied cyrus therefore keepe woman bidde see well vnto paraduenture taken good tyme thei departed yonge gentleman markyng singulare beautie ladie perceiuyng greate honestie hauyng custodie thought would dooe pleasure gesture sawe ingrate vnthakfull verie diligent part cause seruauntes thinges comyng redie chaunce sicke lacked kepyng vpon whiche occasios fell loue meruell saied woman verie faire amiable afterwardes kyng cyrus desirous sende spie countrie lydia learne assirians araspas whiche kepyng faire ladie seemed moste meete purpose araspas chauced fall loue ladie suche wise forced breake mynde must needes satisfie pleasure whiche request like faithfull louing woman housbande absence denied howbeit would accuse araspas cyrus beyng afraied sette variaunce betwene twoo frendes araspas thinkyng greate shame reproche vnto hym obtaine desire threatened ladie would yelde requeste would haue perforce woman fearyng violence kepte thyng longer secrete sente one eunuch cyrus commaundyng hym discouer whole matter whiche heard laughed good pace saied superiour loue sendyng artabasus eunuche commaunde hym force woman could faire meanes allure would artabasus came araspas rebuked hym bothe infidelitie thyng committed vnto charge also wickednesse iniurie incontinecie wherewithall araspas wepte sorowe beyng oppressed shame confounded feare displeasure cyrus whiche thing cyrus vnderstandyng called hym priuelie saied thus vnto hym see araspas afraied muche ashamed contente knowe goddes haue vanquished loue dooe vnderstande thinges wiseste men haue suffred haue accused self bicause could coteine companie faire personage hereof self occasion compelled inuincible matter araspas makyng aunswere saied thing cyrus euen like vnto self mercifull full clemencie mennes reporte whiche maketh moste pensite sone rumour calamitie dispersed mine enemy reioyce frendes counsaill flee lest maiestie doe hainously take reuenge mine offence well araspas saied cyrus opinion brute shall dooe greate seruice emonges confederate said araspas therein doe seruice presently q cyrus doe make though fledde goyng vnto myne enemy maie winne greate credite uerely saied araspas suppose frendes might raise rumour deede fledde feare maie saied cyrus returne vnto v knowe enemy secretes thinke thei make priuie al counsell aduises bicause shalbe incredite nothyng shalbe cocealed desire knowe euen depart said araspas verie likely departure maie seme bee argumente trouthe bicause fledde feare punishment maner forsake faire panthea q cyrus truely saied euidentlie appereth endewed two mindes one haue plaied philosopher loue vntrue sophistre one minde whiche good badde one tyme loueth good euill thinges one instant perpetrate doe one thing wherefore manifest twoo myndes good minde ruleth dooeth thynges honest euill superiour woorketh ill good mynde makyng frende confederate doeth puissauntlie gouerne well saied cyrus goe must beware credite maie increase emonges tell hardely indeuours suche wise doynges maie bee lettes enterprise shall let muche saie determine inuade countrie hearyng thei assemble whole power euery man fearyng priuate parte see tary good space looke partes thei meane nerest approche conuenient v knowe bidde redie soeuer thei thinke time shall departed thought knowe order thei must needes keepe bee fraied alter whiche thei doe thei confounde selues sodaine chaunge thus araspas departyng tellyng moste trustie seruauntes would haue dooen matter went waie panthea hearyng araspas gone sent cyrus saiyng sorie cyrus departure araspas enemy suffer sende husbande doe promise shalbe farre assured frende araspas knowe come greate power aide able make father assirian kyng whiche raigneth frende king vpon tyme went make diuorcement betwene husbande therefore knowyng kyng dooeth disdaine good fortune sure would sone bee perswaded serue noble prince cyrus hearyng saie commau ded sende husband whiche abradatas knowyng wiues token vnderstanding effecte message spedely came cyrus horseman thei persian spy sent cyrus declaryng cyrus commaunded forthwith shuld brought vnto wife whe wife husbande sawe eche thei imbrased like twoo mette suche troublesome aduenture panthea declared goodnes temperaunce clemencie cyrus towarde abradatas hearyng interteignemente saied shall dooe panthea render thankes cyrus thyng saied panthea indeuour self suche trustie frende hym hath towardes abradatas went cyrus sawe hym tooke hym right hande saied pleasure haue doen cyrus haue saie assure self vnto frende seruaunt confederate soeuer see desire shall imploye self vttermoste power aide helpe cyrus said accept tyme dismisse goe suppe wife shall againe bee placed lente frendes myne abradatas sawe preparacion cyrus made enemy addressed make prouision hymself wife panthea made treasure curate helmet gold likewise vambrace furnished horsses chariot brasen barbes cyrus made diuers oracions incoragyng armie taken order thynges might prosperouslie succede diuidyng capitaines seuerall battailes appoinctyng euery charge abradatas shewed hymself verie braue martiall chariot aboute put linen breast plate accordyng countrie maner wife panthea gallante braue capitaine whose nature complexion agreed comelinesse takyng raines chariot handes prepared hymself mounte vp panthea beeyng commaunded stande backe saied truely abradatas woman esteme noble manne liue shame esteme beste self worst greate thankes owe cyrus princelie interteignemente beyng captiue chosen like prisoner shame free without spot blemish mine honor vsed though brother woordes goddes giuen thee bodie accordyng immoderate desire thy minde whole worlde could able hold thee one thy handes thou wouldest touche oriente thy hande occident thou haste gotten thou wilte desire knowe brightnesse diuine maiestie placed thus thou couetest thing thou art able receiue europa thou marchest asia asia thou passest europa afterwardes thou doest vanquishe mankinde thou must make warre wooddes snowes riuers wilde beastes doest thou knowe greate tree growe long yet rooted grounde moment foole looketh fruict doeth measure height tree whereon groweth take hede lest thou doest contende clim toppe thou fallest downe bowes whiche thou doest imbrace lion also somtyme made feede smallest birdes rust consumeth iron nothyng firme perill weake haue doe thee wee neuer touched thy lande thou art whence commest lawfull v ignoraunte liue waste wooddes subiecte manne desire rule wee haue certaine giftes peculiar vnto v thou shalte ignoraunte state nacion yoke tren plough dart bowle thinges vse bothe fre de againste enemy unto frendes wee giue fruictes gotten labour ox bowle sacrifice wine goddes enemy strike dart farre speare nere hande sorte time past ouercame kyng scythia afterwardes kyng medium persia waie open vnto v aegipt thou whiche doest boaste thou art come persecute theues art common thefe nacions wherevnto thou makest thy repaire countrie lydia thou haste taken thou hast enioyed syria thou doest possesse persia bactrianes vnder thy power thou dooest goe india thou extendest thy vnstable gredie handes vpon cattall nede haste thou rich whiche doe make thee hungrie thou art first men whiche sacietie hast gotten famine thou haste gredelie thou couetest thynges thou hast doest thou remember long thou hast slicked bactria while thou goest aboute bryng subiection sogdians beginne reuolte thus warre dooeth growe vnto thee thy victorie bee thou neuer great puissant ouer yet none induce gouerned stranger passe tanais thou shalt perceiue breadth beareth yet thou shalt neuer ouertake scithians whose pouertie swifter thy armie whiche carieth spoile many nacions thou shalt thinke v farre thou shalte see v within thy campe like swiftnesse folowe flee awaie heare desertes voide place mocked greke prouerbes couet rather desertes place vnhabited city plentifull soiles therfore holde faste thy fortune tickle bee holden folowe thou counsaile good specially while tyme doeth serue bridle thy felicitie thou shalt rule better coutrie saie fortune without feete hath onely handes winges whe stretcheth forth hand suffer winges touched finally thou god thou oughtest giue benefites mortall menne take awaie commodity thei haue alredie thou man consider thou art alwaie thou art foolishe parte remember thinges forget thy self people fele thy warres thou maiest vse thy fredes frendship moste firme stable emonges equall seme bee equall haue vsed force violence emonges themselues beware thou take thy fredes thou doest subdue bring obedience frendship betwene maister seruaunte peace lawe armes obserued beleue scythian doe binde frendship othe thei make othe obseruacion faithe maner grekes iustifie factes inuocacion goddes witnesse wee knowe religion consisteth faithe self thei whiche doe renerence men doe begile goddes thou haste nede hym thy frende whose frendship thou stadest doubt thou haste v kepers asia europa wee touche countrie bactria tanais whiche deuideth v beyonde tanais al farre thracia fame thracia bordreth vpon macedonia wee beyng neighbour bothe thy dominion chose whether wilte haue v frended foe woordes sentence maried state doeth vtter proclame ye romanes could without wiues wee wante griefe bicause nature hath prouided neither wee liue passe tyme conuenientlie yet meanes without satisfied ought rather make preparacion perpetuall health short pleasure whiche woordes diuers romanes displeased founde faulte metellus went aboute exhorte people mariage ought meanes confesse griefes incommodities censor rhetorician like one professed rhetorike giuen rhetorician vse false sentence bolde subtile capcious thei likelie maie action moue harte men moreouer saied shame rhetorician euill matter leaue taught hym vttermoste knowledge scholer euathlus defraude hym reste money determined neuer aduocate whose craft protagoras perceiuyng cited hym write appere iudge answere rest bargaine thei bothe come iudges presence protagoras spake scholer wise euathlus bargain betwene v thou canst chose confesse acknowledge whiche effecte agreed teache thee arte pleadyng first matter whiche thou diddest pronouce sentence giuen thy parte thou shouldest paie halfe money firste moitie receiued hande auoide satisfaction thereof although thou knowest haue full well deserued thou defraude duetie refusest bee aduocate tell thee thy determinacion vaine frustrate haue intangled thee suche nettes thou canste escape one meane thou shalte forced paie iudge doe condempne thee mangre thy head thou shalt constrained contrarie wise sentece giuen thy side thou shalte likewise bounde paie thy verie couenaunt sitheus thou art boud therevnto thou pleadest first sentence giuen thy behalf doe thou list fine thou shalt forced paie despite thy teeth assistauntes helde protagoras affirming suite verie reasonable notwithstandyng euathlus bolde spirite aunswered hymself maner sir protagoras semeth vnto vsed discourse matter shall fall sentence giue side bargaine made betwene v voide none effecte bicause losyng profit first pleadyng wherein agrement sentence giue behalfe bargaine accoplished bee beholdyng partes yonge gentlemannes bodie perceiuyng signe sicknes either vrine accidente wherby could iudge bodie diseased many discourse gaue iudgemente infirmitie proceded passion minde whiche yongeman actife valiaunt liued tyme therewithall verie beautifull comelie whiche made hym bee beloued men father continually chamber quene self oftentymes visited hym owne handes serued hym meates drinkes whiche bicause phisteio knowe whether fame yonge man pleasure whether hurt good suppose sight ioyfull vnto hym placed coforte hope quietnesse delight beholding eye many time beautie greatlie desired enioye hearyng speake occasion death receiuyng seruice meates drinkes hades loued better balles eye vnto durste make requeste praier whether grief surmounted aud therefore continually pined consumed thinke reason bee beleued doubteth felyng hymself bee touched delicate handes seyng sitte hym many tymes sake fetche many sighes suche sweete woordes bidde hym bet good aud wanted thyng tell praied hym pleasaunt wordes call lacked sake would gladlie accomplish desire doubteth saie merueilouslie tormented thousande cogitacions conceiuyng hope dispaire still concludyng hymself rather die manifest loue grief yonge men bee thei neuer meane base codicion youthlie tyme lose life shall thinke antiochus beyng yongman freshe flourishyng age sonne riche mightie kyng looked might escape death father heire al willingly craue death small disease assured sorowe infinite antiochus beaten pitie loue hope desire fatherly reuerence thousande thynges like ship tossed depe sea litle litle bega thought many tymes wise graue menne ire hatred disdaine malinconie affection could easilie faine dissemble passion loue kept secrete doeth close kepyng thereof greater hurte made manifeste albeit antiochus could learne cause loue yet imaginacion entred hedde purposed finde continuall abode hym greate diligence obserue marke action aboue take heede mutacion poulses wherevpon beatyng alter deliberacion purposed sat downe bedde side tooke antiochus arme helde fast poulses ordinarily doe beate chaunced instant quene stratonica entred chamber sone yonge man sawe comyng towarde sodainlie contiuned chamber beatyng quicke liuelie departed ceased wonted weaknes poulces retourned long quene came againe chaber soner espied antiochus poulces receiued vigor bega leape still continued whe departed force vigor poulce departed also noble phisicion seyng mutacion still chaunced vpo presence quene thought founde occasion antiochus sickenesse determined better marke next daie assured morowe erasistratus sat doun againe yonge gentleman toke hym arme poulce made mocio king came se sonne yet poulses still beholde quene came soner sodainlie thei reuined yelded suche liuelie mouyng would haue said yonder setteth harte fire beholde life death erasistratus well assured certaine antiochus feruently inflamed mother lawe shame constrained hym conceale hotte firebrandes tormented hym keepe close secrete certified opinion would open matter considered waie best giue knowledge therof kyng seleucus well debated matter deuised waie knewe seleucus loued wife beyonde measure also antiochus dere vnto soonnes healthe yea though cost good realme wise bee gotten die shall doe kyngdome wherevnto erasistratus answered like grace sone loue wife bicause loue semeth vnto disco uenient dareth manifest shame rather wisheth die ope minde howbeit certaine euident signes doe wei perceiue seleucus heard woordes saied erasistratus thou beyng worthie man fewe goodnesse humilitie comparable dere welbeloued beareth bruite verie hauen harborough wisedome wilt thou saue sonne whiche yonge man vpon floure youth worthie life empire asia worthelie reserued erasistratus soonne thy frende seleucus thy kyng loue silence poineted death thou seest modestie honestie sake laste doubtfull passage rather chose die speakyng offende thee wilte thou helpe hym silence discrecion reuerence whiche sheweth ought moue thee copassion thinke welbeloued erasistratus loue ardently forced loue vndoubtedlie could loue would best could loue yea endeuour resist able prescribe lawes loue loue knowe onelie forceth men also commaudeth immortall goddes thei bee able resist mannes pollicie preuaile wherfore knoweth pitie mine dere antiochus dooeth deserue beyng constrained none otherwise doe silent loue moste euident signe noble rare vertue dispose thy minde therefore helpe soonne assure thee thou dooe loue life antiochus seleucus life muste needes bee hated thee bee hurte likewise must hurted wise phisicion seyng aduise came passe thought seleucus instant vpon hym healthe sonne better proue minde intencion spake vnto hym wise common saiyng moste dradde soueraigne lorde man hole ca giue hym sicke weake verie condicion kepte companie suspicion thei rode together familiarly talkyng good felowes seyng marchant thinkyng money determined robbe hym thei sawe aduauntage intente suspect nothyng thei rode like graue men honest conuersacion debatyng hym honest thynges faithfull shewyng themselfes well thei could lowlie gentle upon whiche occasio thought hymself moste happie haue mette suche companie bicause accustomed make whe ride waie rinaldo answered tell truthe man verie plain rude matter haue fewe praiers finger endes suche myne auncestours vsed lette go currant ii xxiiiid neuerthelesse haue alwaies vsed ride waie saie mornyng goyng forthe lodgyng pater noster aue maria soule ye father mother sainct iulian afer praie god saincte iulian sende good lodgyng night folowyng full ofte tyme haue founde traueilyng country many greate daungers whiche hauyng escaped hath fortune alwayes night approched chaunce vpon good honeste lodgyng whiche maketh sted fastlie beleue saincte iulian vnto whose honour saie hath obteined benefite god thought daie wherein neglected saie mornynge praier could neither sauflie trauell ne yet night obtaine good harborough demaunded question asked hym hast thou saied mornyng yea verelie answered rinaldo whiche alredie knewe matter would goe said thou shalte haue enough doe anon thou haue said mornyng maie hap thou shalt lodge full il night afterwards saied haue likewise traueiled day great waie yet neuer saied praiers haue heard many men greatly praise yet could neuer perceiue haue well lodged peraduenture nighte shall proue whiche v twoo shall haue best lodging whiche haue saied whiche haue said moste true haue accustomed steede praier saie verse dirupisti antheme intemerata deprofundis whiche graunde mother teache instructe verie greate force vertue speakyng thus diuers thinges alwaies ridyng expectyng place time put wicked intent effecte chaunced approchyng nere castelll guglielmo thei passed ouer riuer three theues late euening darke place sette vpon hym robbed hym dismountyng horsse left shurte thei goyng awaie thei saied vnto hym goe seeke thy sainct iulia helpe thee good lodging nighte saincte helpe v good passyng riuer thei went waie seruaunt rinaldo perceiuing theues sette vpon maister like cowarde helped hym nothing tournyng bridle neuer lefte gallopyng vntill came castell guglielmo bicause night lodged hymself inne whithout care master rinaldo still shurte barefooted bare legged greate frost snowe knowyng dooe seyng night alredie approche quaking teethe clacketyng head began looke could see place hym resort succour might die cold seyng none al bicause alitle warres fire cosumed thinges beyng sore afflicted colde beganne runne towardes castell guglielmo knowing al seruaunt fled thither thinkyng might come god would sende succor darke night ouertoke good way culd come castell almoste space mile whiche meanes arriued verie late gate shutte vp bridge drawen could goe reason whereof sorowefull discomforted lamentablie castyng eye espie wer possible lest might shroude hymself free snowe chaunce sawe house vpon walles castell vnder whiche determined rest hymself till daie repairyng thither fofide vnder house doore whiche locked vnder whiche doore gathered litle straw founde sat doune verie heauie pensife making complaint many tymes vnto saincte iulian saiyng faithe whiche reposed deceiued hym saincte iulian taking pitie vpon hym vithout delaie prepared hym good lodgyng dwelled castell woman whiche widowe faire persone might seen marque azzo loued life kept pleasure woman dwelt house vnder porche wherof rinaldo gone rest daie chauce marque came thither disport hymself night house secretlie caused bathe bee made commaunded greate supper prepared thinges beyng redie goodwife expectyng nothyng el commylig marque chaunced one menne called gate castell brought suche newes marque sodainly must ride awaie wherefore sent woorde widowe attende commyng litle displeased newes knowyng doe determined entre bathe whiche prepared marque supped goe bedde bathe hard dore poore rinaldo approched widowe beyng bathe bearyng plaintes tremblyng voice made rinaldo thoughte noise storke wherefore called maide said vnto goe vp looke ouer walles see doore knowe would haue maide accordyng maistres commaudement nighte beyng somewhat cleare sawe rinaldo sittyng shurt bare legged shaking colde saied wherevpon asked rinaldo teethe shiueryng heade could scarse well speake vtter woorde brieflie could tolde purpose come thither afterwardes piteously beganne praie could suffer hym night sterue colde maide pitiyng estate returned maistres tolde sawe like wise hauyng compassion vpo remembring keye doore whiche sometymes serued turne marque disposed secretly come saied maide goe open doore softlie haue prepared supper man eate also lodging sufficient harbour hym maide greatlie praisyng maistres curtesie wente forthe opened doore let thei perceiued hym bee almoste frosen colde saiyng vnto dispatche good felowe goe bathe beyng yet hotte whiche thyng right willingly lokyng hidden againe beyng recomforted warmeth thereof felt hymself reuiued death life good wife caused certaine apparell late deade husbande bee searched hym put thei mete though thei made purpose waityng please good wife commaunde hym began humblie thanke god sainct iulian deliuered euill night contrary expectacion brought good lodgyng faier widowe litle reposyng self caused great fire made one greate chamber whiche came demaunded maide maner manne whereto maide answered saiyng maistres good apparell verie handsome manne semeth good reputacion honestie goe thy way quod maistres call hym hither bidde hym come fire tell hym shall suppe perchaunce hath eate meate night rinaldo came chamber seyng widowe made greate reuerence thankyng kindnesse shewed vnto hym widowe seen hym heard speake perceiuyng hym suche one maide reported receiued hym curteous wise causyng hym familierly sitte doune fire demaunded mishappe brought hym place rinaldo rehersed whole discourse heard commyng rinaldo seruaunt castell reporte robberie whiche made beleue better tolde hym also man come toune might easily finde next mornyng meate serued table rinaldo washed together satte doune supper goodlie personage faier pleasaunte beholde yonge good behauiour vpon woman many tymes caste eye liked well shorte lecherous ladie burnyng inwardlie amourous desire abused self hym steede marque morning began shewe forthe light widowe intent suspicion might gaue certain base course apparell filled purse money praiyng hym kepe secrete firste tolde hym whiche waie goe seeke man lettyng hym doore whereat came semyng though traueiled great waie mornyng gate opened wente castell founde seruaunt wherfore puttyng vpo hym suche apparell male beeyng aboute gette vp vpon mannes horsse came passe like diuine miracle three theues whiche robbed hym night taken doyng robberie thei comitted litle wer brought castell vpon confession horsse apparell money restored hym againe losing nothyng paire garter wherefore rinaldo thankyng god iulian mounted vpon horse retourned hole saufe owne house nexte daie three theues conueied forthe blesse worlde heeles three yonge menne hauyng fondlie consumed thei became verie poore whose nephewe retourned englande italie waie fill acquaintaunce abbotte vpon familiaritie knewe bee kyng englandes doughter whiche toke husbande afterwardes restored vncles loss sent home good state reputacion pthe xxxiiij nouell somtime citie florence knight called sir tebaldo saie house lamberti affirme agolanti leauyng variaunce whether house true time notable riche wealthie knight three sonnes firste called lamberto seconde tebaldo thirde agolante faire goodlie child eldest xviij yeres age saied sir tebaldo died lawfull heires left landes goodes seyng themselfes verie riche redie money possession cotinued life without gonernement owne pleasure without bridle staie thei began consume goodes thei kepte greate francke house many horsses greate value dogges haukes sundrie kindes continuallie kept open house giuyng liberall giftes obseruyng diuerse gestes tilt torney thing onelie appertaine belong gentlemenne also whiche incident trade course youthe thei continued longe order substaunce lefte father verie muche consumed reuenues able maintaine expences began decrease wherevpon thei faine morgage sell inheritaunce suche wise ende thei grewe extreme pouertie penurie ope eye like sort richesse closed vp cause lamberto vpon daie call twoo brother vnto hym tolde honour father value richesse amounte pouertie thei wer come disordinate expences giuyng counsaill well coulde miserie growe vpo sellyng whiche left thei goe waie whiche thei without leaue taken man solempnitie thei departed florence taried place thei arriued englande takyng litle house citie london thei liued litle expences began lende money vsurie fortune fauourable vnto trade fewe yeres thei gained verie notable money whiche made one retire againe florence substaunce thei redemed greate parte inheritaunce bought lande gaue themselues mariage continewing neuerthelesse england money interest thei sente thither factour yonge manne nephewe called alexandro thei three dwellyng still florence began againe forget miserie inordinate expences broughte albeit thei charged housholde yet thei spente order without respecte greate credite euery marchaunte whose expences money alexandro many tymes sende home helpe supporte certaine yeres whiche lente diuerse gentleman baron countrie vpon castelles manours reuenues whereof receiued incredible profite meane tyme three brother spent largelie thei borowed money fixyng hope englande chaunced contrary opinion al men warres happened betwene kyng england one sonnes whiche bredde muche diuision countrie holdyng one part meanes whereof manours morgaged landes taken awaie alexandro hauyng nothing whervpo profite rise daily trustyng peace concluded betwene father sonne thynges surrendred aswell principall interest determined departe countrie three brother whiche florrence limityng order disordinate expences grewe daily worsse worsse processe tyme hope past recouery thei lost onely credite creditor desirous paied faine sende prison bicause inheritance sufficient paie whole debt thei remained prison rest wiues childre dispersed countrie hether thither order knowing abide poore miserable life euer alexandro whiche long tyme taried peace englande seing would come passe considering hymself ouer besides vaine abode recouery debtes daunger life purposed retourne italie traueiled waie alone departed bruges fortune perceiued abbot clothed white like maner take iourney accompanied many monkes greate traine hauyng muche cariage diuers baggage rode twoo olde knightes kinsmenne kyng alexandro entred acquaintance reason former knowledge receiued companie alexandro ridyng frendly demaunded monkes thei rode greate traine whether thei wente one knightes answered whiche rode yonge gentle man kinsman newlie chosen abbot one best abbaies englande bicause verie yonge lawfull decree suche dignitie thei went rome obteine holie father dispensacion age co firmacion dignitie thei willed hym disclose manne newe abbot riding sometymes sometymes see ordinarilie lordes doe thei trauell countrie chaunced abbot perceiuyng alexandro ridyng besides whiche faire yonge manne honest curteous familier first meting merueilouslie delight thing euer sawe life callyng hym vnto hym began familierlie talke asked whence came whether went alexandro declared liberallie state satisfied demaude offryng vnto hym although power little seruice able dooe abbote hearyng curteous offer comelie talke placed good order consideryng particulerlie state affaire waiyng hym self albeit traine small yet neuerthelesse semed gentleman pitiyng mishappes recomforted hym familierlie saied vnto ought daily liue good hope honeste manne god would aduaunce onelie place fro whence fortune throwen hym doune also greater estimacion praiyng sithes goyng thuscane whether likewise went would please remaine compaine alexandro thanked hym humblie comfort said vnto redie imploie hymself please hym comaunde abbot thus riding whose minde newe thoughtes entred vpon sight alexandro chauced many day iourneis thei arriued village meanlie furnished lodgyng abbot desirous lodge alexandro intreated hym lighte inne hoste whiche familiarly knowen vnto caused chamber made redie hymself worste place house marshall abbottes lodgynges beyng alredie come toune whiche manne verie skilfull affaire lodged traine village one well could time abbot supped night farre spente euery man repaired bedde alexandro demauded host lie hoste made answere trouthe maister alexandro knowe see house full housholde faine lie vpon bench beit haue certaine garrettes harde adioynyng lorde abbottes chamber maie place verie well cause folkes beare thither pallet please maie lodge night alexandro saied shall goe throughe abbottes chamber streighte rome one monkes able lie knowen curteins drawen would haue caused monkes haue lien garrette selfe would haue lodged thei dooe wherevnto hoste saied dooen thinke maie liste lie well place house abbot beyng slepe curteins drawen hym softlie without noise conueie pallett thithere alexandro perceiuyng might doen without anoyaunce abbot agreed conueied secretlie could chamber abbot slepe gaue thinke imagine vpon newe desire hearde woordes spoken betwene hoste alexandro likewise vnderstanding alexandro laie verie well contente began saie lorde hath sente time fauourable satisfie desire whiche receiue peraduenture like neuer bee offred againe wherefore perswading take present occasio supposing likewise euery slepe called alexadro softlie could willed come lie beside many excuse clothes came vnto hym abbot laiyng arme ouer began attempte suche amorous toy accustomed betwene twoo louers whereof alexandro merueiled muche doubted abbotte beyng surprised dishonest loue called hym bedde purpose proue hym whiche doubte abbot either presumption acte dooen alexandro vnderstandyng continentlie beganne smile putte shurte whiche ware tooke alexandros hande laied ouer stomacke saiyng vnto hym alexandro cast thy minde thy vnhonest thoughte fele thing whiche haue secrete alexandro laiyng hande ouer abbottes stomack perceiued twoo breastes rounde harde skinne whereof verie fine neshe whereby perceiued woman incontinentlie embraced without looking inuitacio would haue kissed saied vnto thou approche nerer marke shall saie vnto thee woman man thou maiest perceiue beyng departed maide house goyng pope praie place mariage whe first viewed thee daie whether thy good fortune mishappe loue attached suche wise neuer woman loued manne dooe thee therefore dooe purpose take thee husbande others thou wilte take wife get thee hence retourne thine owne bedde alexandro although knewe yet hauyng regarde vnto companie traine followed iudged noble riche ladie parte sawe personage right beautifull faire therefore without consideracion answered somuche pleasure verie well conteted sitting vp bedde hauing litle table wherin picture christ painted indowed ringe order espousalles afterwardes embracing one greate contentacion pleasure thei ioyfullie continued together night thei deuised concluded thorder meanes accomplishe affaire time forthe alexa dro sone daie rose went cha ber waie came without knowledge man laie night right ioifull glad proceded iourney abbotte copanie within fewe day arriued rome thei remained certaine tyme abbot taking twoo knightes alexandro wente pope doyng due reuerence abbot began speake wise holie father holinesse dooeth better knowe euery manne purposeth liue honeste life ought auoide muche lieth occasios maie drawe cotrary whiche thintent desirous leade honeste life maie fullie performe secretlie fledde arriued habite wherein see good porcion kyng englandes treasure father holinesse maie bestowe mariage muche father would giue wife whiche yonge gentlewoman see scottishe king verie riche wealthie prince olde age muche occasion departure feare conceiued place mine eye gracious mercie truste thinketh meete bee husbande whiche yonge gentleman poinetyng alexandro see standing besides honestie worthinesse well able match greate ladie honourable euer bee although peraduenture nobilitie bloudde excellent procedeth roiall princelie stocke haue chosen husbande haue none whatsoeuer father shall faie cotrarie wherefore principall occasion moued come hither foistes galleis turkes recouered onelie whiche lost marchadize also twise muche wherevnto loss amounte wherefore well punished firste sorowe loss knowyng gaines multiplie neded retourne seconde tyme thought whiche gotten sufficiet therfore determined presetlie returne owne house gotten goodes fearyng hinderaunce susteined traffique marchaudise purposed imploie money longer way barque wherwith gained ore tooke course homeward beyng vpon maine sea night winde rose southeast onelie cotrary course also caused suche tempest smalle barque able indure sea wherevpon tooke harborough creke sea whiche compassed litle islande expectyng better winde whiche creke within muche doe auoidyng tempest arriued twoo greate argoseis genoa wer come constantinople mariner whiche shippes thei sawe litle barque shut vp way could goe vnderstandyng whence knowyng reporte verie riche determined beyng ikenne naturallie giuen spoile loue money take settyng shore parte meune well armed furnished crossebowes thei conueied theselfes keepe defende none within pinna excepte would shot able escape retiryng skiftes helpe tide thei approched landolpho barke without great difficultie smalle space thei tooke companie losyng muche one manne cariyng landolpho aborde one cockes within borde litle pinna thei soncke mariner kepte landolpho sufferyng haue kinde armure muche haberion next daie winde chaunged shippes hoisted vp sailes toward leuant daie prosperouslie sailed voiage vpon closyng night storme rose separated twoo shippes one force winde chaunced shippe wherein poore landolpho strake greate violence vpon sande islande cephalonia one would throwe glasse wall euen shippe opened fill peces whereby sorowfull mariner stoode aboue sea beyng couered gooddes coaffers planckes shippe swame aboue water whiche chaunceth many tymes suche like accidentes night beyng darke billowes goyng high ble suche able swimme began take holde thinges whiche fortune gaue vnto emonges wretched landolpho seyng death face whiche greatlie desired many tymes craued daie rather retourne home poore estate afraied taught holde borde amonges reste trustyng might chaunce god would pardon hym drownyng sende hym refuge escape horsebacke fletyng vpon plancke well could driuen sea winde helde fast fame till daie light whiche perceiued looked aboute hym sawe nothyng cloudes sea coaffer swimmyng aboue water whiche driuen nere hym made hym many tymes feare would bee ouerthrowe nerer came laboured putte backe well could hande although force power gone euer chaunced gale winde blewe sky strake coaffer againste borde wherevpon landolpho meanes driue backe forced giue ouer plack billowe beaten vnder water afterwardes remountyng lofte againe swamme feare force seyng borde caried farre hym fearyng lest bee able fasten drewe toward coafer whiche nere inough vnto laiyng breast vpon couer thereof made goe right could armes maner driue sea without eating hauyng wherewithall drinkyng would continued daie night folowing knowyng sawe nothyng sea nexte mornyng either god windes force ladolpho whiche transformed sponge holdyng faste bothe handes brimme coafer like se feare bee drouned dooe take holde nexte thyng cometh hande arriued shore af isle corfu fortune poore woman scowryng vessell sande salte water seyng hym drawe nere perceiuing forme fashion man afraied criyng ranne backe able speake se verie litle could saie nothyng sea droue hym nere shore woman discried likenes coafer beholdyng aduisedlie sawe length armes vpon therewithall face merueilyng self wherfore moued compassion went sea litle waie whiche calme catchyng hym heare pluckte coafer lande muche doe vnfolded armes coafer causyng maide carrie coafer vpon bedde bare hym lande like litle childe whiche dooen put hym hotte house warme water frotting rubbyng hym naturall heate sens loste began come againe former course sawe tyme toke hym cherishing comforting wine brothes well could made length recouer force suche wise knewe woman deliuered hym coafer whiche saued hadde hym seke aduenture thus good wife delte landolpho litle estemed coafer yet considered could small valour able beare charge certaine day feelyng light cleare voide hope haue succour relief thereof neuerthelesse good wife doores brake open see within founde many precious iewelles bounde together lose wherin pretie skill knowyng greate value giuyng thankes god whiche yet forsaken hym wholie recomforted howbeit muche litle space twise cruellie distressed tormented fortune fearyng third tyme thought nedefull take hede dispose thinges sauftie till came home owne house wherefore hauing bestowed precious iewelles certaine ragges cloutes well could saied goodwife neede coafer would giue hym bagge would bestowe vpo whiche good wife willinglie landolpho giuyng greate thankes could kindnes whiche founde handes tooke leaue imbarking passed branditio fro thence fro place place till came tranj finding diuers citie wherein dwelte draper apparelled maner god sake tolde discourse fortune except coafer let hym horse sent diuers companie bryng hym home rauello sauftie arriued thanked god brought hym thither searched bougette leasure firste founde many stone great valoure selling price reasonable lesse thei worthe substaunce amount muche departed house founde meanes dispatche sell iewelles sent corfu good pece money woman tooke hym sea recompence kindnesse founde handes like tranj giuen hym apparell rest tooke hymself would marchaunt liued home honeste estate ende life andreuccio perugia come naples buy horsse one night surprised three merueious accidetes whiche hauyng escaped one rubie retourned home house pthe xxxvi nouell perugia ae yong man called andreuccio di pietro horssecorser vnderstading horse faire naples put fiue hundred crounes pursse neuer traueiling owne house wente thither certaine marchauntes arriuyng naples vpon sondaie night nexte mornyng accordyng instruction giuen hosse went faire viewed sawe many horsse whereof diuers verie well like hym demaunded prises none could agree price shewe right well able man paie bought many tymes like dolle foole drewe pursse stuffed crounes presence passed fro chaunced yonge woma scicilia whiche verie faire euery mannes commaundement litle hire passed shewyng pursse marked perceiued andreuccio sodainlie saied selfe toune like vnto al crounes mine passed forth yonge peate olde woman scicilian also sone espied andreuccio forsoke copanion ran affectuouslie imbrace hym whiche yonge woman perceiuing speakyng woorde gaue good heede thei saied andreuccio tournyng olde woman immediatlie knewe reioysed muche happelie mette greate gratulacions many welcome promised visite lodgyng whiche doen departed andreuccio retourned buy horsse howbeit morning bought none yonge dame whiche hadde firste seen pursse marked acquaintaunce betwene olde woman hym assaie meanes might gette money least parte thereof subtellie asked olde woman manne whence knewe old woman particularlie recoumpted whole acquaintaunce dwelt long tyme scicilia father afterwardes perugia likewise tolde retourned cause come naples iollie wenche wholy informed andreuccio parentes name made plat foundacion subtill craftie meanes obtaine purpose come home house sent olde woman businesse daie bicause might retourne andreuccio dwellyng pretie girle well noseled broughte vp doyng arrantes euenyng sent lodgyng andreuccio make inquirie fortune chaunced finde hym standyng alone bostes doore girle aske knewe honest perugia called andreuccio di pietro hosted yes girle quod manne tooke hym side saied vnto hym sir gentle woman toune would gladlie speake wer pleasure whiche andreuccio hearde called mynde semed hymself goodlie yange manne persone without doubte woman loue bicause al naples thought none proper striplyng hymself incontinentlie answered would waite vpon demaunding whe come place made answere euen pleaseth sir maistresse attedeth home andreuccio vpo without woorde spoken hoste whether gone saied wenche goe thou followe girle conducte hym maistres house whiche dwelt streate called malpertugio name shewyng honestie streate dwelte knowyng suspectyng nothyng thought place right honest went vnto wife likewise honest good boldlie entred house wenche goyng mou ting staiers yonge gristle called maistresse saiyng vnto maister andreuccio come redie vpper steppe seemed though attended hym ladie fine good face well apparelled trimmed best maner seing maister andreuccio hande descended twoo steppe staiers armes open imbrace hym foldyng aboute necke paused certaine space without speakyng woorde though greate loue earnest affection enforced doe wepyng kissed face voice halfe vttered betwene howlyng speakyng saied vnto hym andreuccio myne owne dere harte moste hartelie well come andreuccio merueilyng tender woordes amased answered getlewoman also wel founde afterwardes toke hand conueied hym vp parlour thence without talke chamber whiche al perfumed rose flower orenges swete smelles sawe bedde wel furnished diuers sortes apparell placed vpo press accordyng maner countrie many faire riche ornamentes reason whereof andreuccio whiche freshewater souldiour thoughte greate ladie thei twoo sitting together vpon chest beddes feete began thus saie vnto hym andreuccio assured dooe greatlie wonder faire woordes curteous interteignement teares whiche lette falle meruaile althoughe doe knowe peraduenture neuer heard tell declare vnto thyng strasige merueilous tell plaine owne sister saie vnto sith hath pleased lorde god shewe muche grace fauour doe se one brother die although desire see al care dooe call wretched woride spirite comforted releued maie chaunce neuer vnderstoode muche tyme tell whole discourse pietro father dwelte long time wherof possible haue heard report palermo goodnesse frendlie behauior hym yet remaining beare hym singular good frendship emonges whiche loued moffe mother gentlewoman widowe without doubt loue best wise forgettyng loue father brother loue owne honour reputacion thei dealed together thei begatte see afterwardes father mine occasion departe palermo retourned perugia leauing mother behinde yong doughter neuer farre knowe caring either mother wherof father would blame muche cosidering ingratitude towardes mother albeit ought vse towardes muche affection fatherlie loue owne doughter come kitchin maide ne yet basewoman mother otherwise knowyng commit handes moued mere loue bothe self thynges ill dooen long tyme paste easie reprehended amended thus matter went left litle infant palermo growen yeres mother whiche riche gaue wife one house gergenti gentleman greate honestie reputacion loue mother retourned dwell palermo greatlie sauoryng faccion guelphi began practise certaine enterprise kyng charles whiche knowen kyng federic enterprise could take effecte forced flie scicilia tyme thought haue chiefest ladie euer island wherefore taking v suche fewe thinges able carie fewe maie well call respecte possessed leauyng house pallaces came vnto citie founde kyng charles benigne towardes v hath recompenced parte loss whiche wee susteined seruice hath giuen v possession house good prouision housholde husbande brother lawe see perceiue maner doe remaine swete brother thake god presente see therewithall tooke hym aboute necke wepyng tenderly kissed face againe andreuccio hearyng tale
