prompt willyng loue seyng tender teares imbracynges honest kiss thought al spoken bee moste certaine true hadde doe tale answered wise madame maie thinke vnkindnesse dooe meruaile verie deede haue acquaintance neuer borne whether father hath spoken mother tyme truely doe reme ber muche dooe reioyce haue founde sister trust bicause alone certainly knowe none honourable maie seme agreable vnto hym well poore marchaunte howbeit doe beseche tell knowe citie answered mornyng poore woman whiche oftentymes repaireth house gaue knowledge thereof bicause longe tyme tolde dwell father palermo perugia bicause thought conuenient mete bid home myne owne house seke mannes thought good sende woordes began order inquire state parentes callyng proper name wherevnto andreuccio made answer perceiued better cause giue credite vnto woordes discourse talke thynges beyng long weather hot called greke wine comfittes made andreuccio drincke banquette destrous departe lodgyng supper time meanes would suffer makyng though angrie saied vnto hym oh god see moste euidently doe make litle accompt beyng owne sister neuer sawe house vnto ought resort euer come towne forsake suppe inne trouth shall chose take part supper although husbande bee home whereof right sorie yet shal knowe wife able make good andreuccio knowyng well saie el made answere loue ought loue sister go mine iune knowe thei tarie night thei goe supper greate reproche shame praised bee god quod haue seruauntes aduertise hoste intent shall tarie pleaseth sir dooe greate curtesie maie sende companion hither beare companie afterwardes needes depart ye maie goe together andreuccio answered would sende none companie night much importunate hymself right well contente satisfie requeste made though sente inne giue worde thei tarie muche communication supper placed vpon table serued many deuises sundrie delicates abundantlie like sleightes continued supper till darke night whe thei rose table andreuccio made hast departe would suffre hym tellyng hym naples towne straight order none might walke abrode night specially strau gers like sente woorde howe thei tary hym supper euen doen bedde whiche andreuccio beleuyng takyng pleasure sister deceiued though false belief well contented tarie talke communicacion supper purpose dilated protracted one part night beyng spent left andreuccio cha ber goyng bedde litle boie waite vpon hym see lacked nothing woman went chaber tyme yere verie hotte wherefore andreuccio beyng alone striped hymself laied hose dublette vnder beddes head desirous goe priuie asked boie poinctyng doore corner chamber saied vnto hym goe andreuccio saufly went chaunced fortune sette foote vpon borde whiche bothe endes lose ioiste wherevpon laie reason wherof borde tombled doune iakes god loued hym fall receiued hurt although good heigth sauyng unbroined arraied doge place wherof iakes ful whiche place intent maie better vnderstande saied shall folowe euen describe vnto litle straighte entrie many tymes see betwene twoo house certain bordes laied vpo twoo ioistes betwene one house upon whiche placed seate priuie one whiche bordes fill downe andreuccio beyng bottome iakes sorowfull sodain chaunce cried boie helpe boie sone heard fallen went tell maistres ran chamber seke clothes founde money whiche andreuccio like foole without mistrust still caried hym possessed thyng whiche laied snare fainyng self bee palermo doughter one perugia caryng longer hym straight waie shutte faste priuie doore whereat went forthe fell andreuccio seyng boie would answere began crie loude vaine wherfore suspecting cause beginnyng somewhat late vnderstande deceipte leapte ouer litle wal closed place fro sight streate open streate wente doore house whiche knewe well enough makyng noise rapping harde long doore vaine whiche cause began complaine lament like vnto one manisfestly sawe misfortune saiyng ala litle tyme haue lost fiue hundred crounes sister many wordes began againe bounse doore crie rapped long cried loude waked many neighbour aboutes able suffer noise rose beddes emoges others one maides house faining self slepie loked windowe saied greate rage noise beneath oh said andreuccio ye knowe andreuccio brother madame floredelice thou haste dronke muche thinketh q maide go slepe come morow knowe none called andreuccio yet vnderstand thou meanest foolishe woordes get thee hence good man lette v slepe praie thee quod andreuccio dooest thou heare saie thou knowest well inough thou wilte scicilian kindred bee sone forgotten giue clothes whiche haue lefte behinde goe hence al harte whereat maide laughed saied thincke man dreame tourned self shutte faste windowe andreuccio sure certaine loss attached incredible sorrowe conuerted anger rage thought recouer anoiaunce whiche could gette faire wordes wherefore takyng vp bigge stone beganne againe greater blowes beate doore whiche whe many neighbour waked slepe risen heare thinkyng troublesome man fained wordes anoye good wife house thei likewise troubled noise lookyng windowes beganne rate hym one voice like sorte curres one streate whiche dooe baule barke straunge dogge passeth saiyng muche shame villanie come house honest wome tyme night speake suche fonde woordes wherefore good man gette thee hence goddes sake let v slepe thou haue thing doe good wife come againe morowe disquiet v nighte whiche wordes poore andreuccio somewhat appeased one within house russian kept good wife andreuccio neuer sawe heard looked windowe bigge horrible voice demaunded beneath whereat andreuccio liftyng vp heade sawe one farre could perceiue seemed bee large rubber blacke bearde sterne visage lokyng though newlie risen bedde full slepe gaping rubbing eye andreuccio answered scarfull wise saiyng good wife brother house russian interrupting answere speaking fiercely firste saied knowe thou arte come doune codgell bombaste thee thou shalt able sturre thy self like asse dronken beaste thou art whiche night wilte suffer v slepe wordes tourning hymself aboute shutte windowe diuers neighbor knewe better condicions terrible russian speakyng faire andreuccio saied vnto hym god sake good man departe hence tyme suffer thy self slaine gette thee hece quod say thou haddest warning andreuccio appalled russian woordes sight moued likewise counsale neighbor spake hym thought charitable wise toke waie retourne inne sorowfullest man euer liued greatest despaire losse money turning waie wherin guided litle girle daie anoyed stenche felte aboute hym desirous goe sea side washe hym declined muche left hand takyng waie vp streat called la ruga catellana marching vp highest parte citie chaunce sawe twoo men hym lanthorne light one handes comyng towardes hym auoidyng bicause feared watch ill desposed persones hidde hymself old house harde thei purpose wente verie place one dischargyng hymself certaine instrumentes yron whiche bare vpo backe bothe viewe surueie yrons debatyng diuers thinges touchyng thei talkyng togethers one said meaneth smell foulest stenche euer felt life whe saied lifted vp lanthorne espied miserable andreuccio couchyng behinde wall afraied asked andreuccio helde peace thei approchyng nere light demaunded made filthely arraied andreuccio rehersed whole aduenture chauced consideryng cause misfortune saied one doubt doen house scarabone butta fuoco tournyng towardes androuccio one saied vnto hym good manne although thou hast loste thy money yet thou hast greate cause praise god thy chaunce falle entre house thou haddest fallen assure thy self thou haddest slepe thy throte cutte thy money shouldest haue lost thy life auaileth wepe lamente thou shaite sone plucke starres elemente euer recouer one penie thy losse without doubt kill thee vnderstande thou make woordes thereof thei saied giuen hym admonicion thei coforted hym wise good felowe doe lament thy state therefore thou wilte ioyne thy self v enterprise whiche haue hande warraunte thee thou shalte gette great deale thou hast lost andreuccio like one extreame despaire contente date buried one messer philippo minutulo archebishoppe naples riche pontificalles ornamentes rubie vpon finger worthe fiue hundreth ducattes golde thei purposed robbe dispoile telling andreuccio whole order intente coueitous well aduised went going towardes greate churche andreuccio persume began sente verie stronge wherevpon one saied possible deuise awaie shitten beaste maie washe hymself place stincke thus filthelie yes quod pitte harde ouer whiche hangeth pulley greate bucket maie presently washe hym thei come pitte thei founde rope hangyng still vpo pulley bucket taken awaie wherefore thei thought beste tye hym rope lette hym doune pitte washe washed wagge rope thei would hoiste hym vp whiche thei chaunced while thus clensyng pitte watche citie thei swette nighte verie hot drie thirstie came pitte drincke twoo perceiuyng watche hande left andreuccio pitte ranne awaie watche whiche come thither drinke perceiued twoo fledde andreuccio beyng still bottome clensed hymself beganne wagge rope watche sittyng doune pittes side caste clokes laied doune halbardes weapon began drawe vp rope thinkyng bucket full water tiede andreuccio haled vp brincke pitte forsoke rope cast hymself one handes vpon side watche sawe thei feare ranne awaie faste thei could without speakyng worde whereof andreuccio meruaile muche taken good holde fallen doune bottome greate hurte peraduenture without perill life notwithstandyng beyng pitte findyng halberdes weapon whiche knewe well fellowes brought began muche wonder betwene feare ignoraunce whiche happened complainyng hymself harde fortune without touchyng thing determined goe thence wente could tell whether departyng place mette fellowes retiryng backe drawe hym vp thei perceiued hym alredie haled pitte thei wonderfully abashed asked drewe hym andreuccio made answere could tell rehearsyng order chaunced thynges founde without thei vnderstandyng matter laughed tolde hym cause wherfore thei ranne awaie thei drewe hym vp without talke beyng midnight thei repaired greate churche whiche thei easely entred wente tombe whiche marble verie huge weightie couer whereof beyng verie greate crowes yron tooles thei lifted vp farre one man able entre whiche doen one asked goe quod one quod quod andreuccio thother twoo hearyng andreuccio saie stepped vnto hym saiyng wilte thou goe faithe owe god thou goe beate thee one yron barres thou shalte neuer sturre againe place andreuccio beeyng made common ridyng foole greatly fearyng heard saie went graue saied vnto hymself good felowes doe make goe bicause thei would deceiue haue giuen redie come thei meane runne awaie saue selfes leaue behinde without part therof wherefore purposed first take owne porcion hymself remembryng rynge great valour whereof thei tolde hym sone graue pulled archbishop finger putte vpon owne afterwardes taking crosse miter gloues dispoiling hym euen shurt gaue saiyng nothyng el thei pressyng vpon hym ring behinde willed hym throughly make serche howbeit still answered could fiude bicause would make tary litle longer fained though made searche subtill malicious badde hym seeke still thei sawe tyme thei toke awaie proppes staied vp tobe ran awaie leauyng poore andreuccio fast shutte graue whiche andreuccio perceiued chaunced hym eche man maie consider assaied sometymes shulders sometyme hedde remoue couer vaine wherefore euen verie sorowe fill sownde vpon deade bodie bishoppe man seen bothe instaunt could well haue discerned whether dead corp archebishoppe dedde poore andreuccio diyng come hymsef began piteouslie complaine seeyng arriued one twoo endes either tombe die hunger stenche dedde body putrifiyng wormes manne came open el hanged thiefe founde within consideracions tormented sorowe heard noyse churche diuerse menne thoughte came dooe like facte fellowes doen wherewith feare began muche augment thei opened graue staied vp came question emo ge goe thei contended good space priest companie saied ye afraied dooe ye thinke eate dedde neuer eate men goe self saied laied hym downe upon breaste drinke graue thrustyng feete wente doune andreuccio seyng erected vpright caught prieste one legges makyng though would haue drawen hym whiche prieste perceiued cried loude speeding fast could wherewithall reste dismaied almoste wittes leauyng graue open tooke legges ranne though hundred thousande deuelles tailes whiche seyng andreuccio ioyfull looked lepte graue ranne fast could churche place came tyme daie light beganne appere ryng finger wandred wist whether till came sea side lengthe recouered inne founde companie hoste night takyng greate care hym recomptyng whiche chaunced hoste gaue hym aduise incontinently gette hym naples whiche presently retourned perugia hauyng bestowed v c crounes vpon ryng whiche thought haue imploied vpon horsses whiche cause made iorney erle angiers beyng falsly accused banished fraunce lefte twoo soonnes sundrie place englande retournyng vnknowen scotlande founde greate aucthoritie afterwardes repaired habite seruaunte frenche kynges armie beyng knowen innocent againe aduaunced firste estate pthe xxxvii nouell romane empire beyng transferred fro frenche menne vnto almanes rose great discencion betwene bothe nacions ende cruell continual warre cause well defence kingdome offede enemy frenche king one soonnes power owne realme frendes ally assembled greate hoste menne encountre enemy thei proceded bicause thei would leaue realme gouernor knowyng gualtieri erle angiers gentle sage knight moste trustie frende man moste expert arte warfare semyng vnto notwithstandyng apt pleasure paine lefte hym lieutenaunt generall place gouernement whole kyngdome fraunce proceded enterprise erle began greate knowledge good order execute office committed vnto hym dooyng nothyng without consente quene faire doughter lawe although thei lefte vnder custodie gouernement yet neuer tholesse honoured maistresses superiours erle gualtieri beautiful personage age fourtie yeres familier well condicioned gentleman could besides moste excellent trimmest knight knowen day one comelie apparell chaunced kyng soone beyng warres aforesaied wife erle died meane leauyng hym onely twoo little yonge child soonne doughter whiche frequentyng courte aforesaied lady talkyng many tymes aboute affaire realme wife kynges sonne fixed eye vpon great affection persone vertues feruentlie imbraced hym secrete loue knowing yonge freshe hym bee without wife thought sodainly bring passe whiche desired thinkyng nothyng could lette onely shame discouer purposed vtterly abandone vpon daie beyng lone sente one seeke erle though would haue communicated hym matter erle whose minde farre different lady incontinently came vnto beyng sette doune together vpon bedde desired alone cha ber asked twise vpon occasion sent hym hauyng nothyng sate vnto pressed ende rapte loue waxed verie shamfast almoste wepyng quakyng feare fainte wordes began saie foloweth derely beloued louyng frende lorde maie easelie knowe beyng wise manne bee frailtie menne woman diuers consideracions weakenesse bee one wherefore iust iudge one fault diuerse quality ought reason receiue one like punishemente moreouer saie poore man woman whiche getteth liuing labor bodie ought bee reprehended thei become amourous subiect lustes riche ladie whiche taketh care liuyng wanteth thyng desireth truely beleue none suche saie whiche reason suppose thinges saied ought serue greatest part excuse aduauntage doeth possesse happe giue self fully conductios loue superplusage said excuse ought consist hath chosen sage vertuous frende loueth hath doen deede whiche twoo thinges thei suppose many also whiche ought induce loue accordynglie youth requireth great space betwene husbande behoueth thei aduaunce themselfes presence defence burnyng loue doe raigne whiche haue power wise beseche giue counsaile aide thing whiche shall demaunde true long absence husbande able resist prickes fleshe force loue whiche suche greate effecte thei haue many time past yet daily doe vaquishe ouercome onely feble weake woman also strongest men liuyng ease idlenes see forced folowe pleasure loue become amourous doe knowe well thynges thei knowen bee repute honest neuerthelesse beyng kepte secrete thinke shall muche dishonest notwithstanding dame loue fauourable vnto onelie hath giuen true iudgement choise frende hath reueiled vnto worthie beloued suche ladie bee greatlie deceiued make accompt fairest personage semeliest curteous wisest gentleman realme fraunce maie saie reason absence without husbande maie affirme bee without wife wherfore beseche ye loue beare vnto wil denie loue frendship wil haue pitie vpon yong yeres whiche doubtles dooe consume ice fierie flame whiche worde teares ran doune suche abundance thought make supplicacion praiers power speake holdyng doune heade like one ouercome threwe self doune erles lappe like faithfull knighte began blame sharpe rebuke fonde foolishe loue pushyng hym clepe hym aboute necke swore greate othes rather would bee drawen fower peces consent suche thyng doen hym honor lorde maister whiche wordes ladie hearyng sodainly forgatte loue greate rage saied vnto hym shall bee frustrate thou arrant villaine wise desired ioye sithens thou goest seke distruction cause thee put death el banished worlde saied caught self heare head almoste tare cleane laied handes vpon garmentes rentyng peces afterwardes cried aloude helpe helpe erle angiers wil rauishe force erle seyng farre doubtyng enuie malice courte owne conscience committed facte fearyng also credite would bee giuen wickednesse ladie innocencie conueied hymself place sone could went palace fledde home owne house without aduise placed child horsebacke well could caried callice brute noyse ladie many people assembled seyng hearyng thoccasion crie onely beleued wordes also affirmed pompouse state erle vsed hym bryng passe effecte desire thei ranne house erle greate furie arreste persone findyng thei first sacked house afterwardes ouerthrewe grounde newes hereof wicked might bee deuised arriued kyng dolphin campe whereat thei troubled offended thei condempned erle progenie perpetuall exile promisyng greate giftes rewardes would presente quicke deade erle beyng offended conscience fledde innocente facte made hymself culpable thereof arriued callice child dissemblyng sodainly passed ouer englande poore apparell traueiled vp london entred citie gaue child diuers admonicions specially two thinges first thei beare paciently pouertie whervnto fortune without offence brought afterwardes wisely thei take heede time manifest declare man whence thei came whose childre thei thei loued price owne liues soonne named lewes almoste age ix yeres doughter called violeta age vij bothe whiche childre age could suffer well obserue father lesson afterwardes right well appere bicause might better brought passe semed good vnto hym alter name namyng soonne perotto doughter gianetta thei arriued lodon maner beggers thei craued almose beyng fortune purpose one mornyng churche doore came passe greate ladie whiche one marshalles englandes wiues goyng churche sawe erle two litle childre beggyng almose demaunded countrie man whether child owne erle answered picarde reason wicked facte dooen eldest soonne vnhappie boie forced departe countrie twoo child ladie whiche pitifull fixed eye vpo girle pleased verie muche bicause beautifull gentill pleasaunt saiyng good man thou contet leaue vnto thy litle doughter whiche hath good face willingly take become duetifull maiden mariageable marie honeste wise demaunde greatly pleased erle redely answered contented teares trickeling doune eye deliuered commended pretie doughter vnto whe thus wel bestowed determined tarrie loger beggyng almose traueiled countrie soonne perotto went wale without greate labour paine one neuer accustomed traueile foote dwelte one kyng englandes marshalles greate aucthoritie kept noble house whose court erle sonne oftentymes repaired practise begge liuyng one marshalles sonnes gentlemennes child doyng certaine childishe sportes pastymes runne leape perotto began entermedle hymself emonges game excellently well none better whiche thyng diuers tymes marshall perceiuing well pleased order childe asked whence told poore mannes soonne whiche many tymes came thither begge almose marshall desiryng childe erle whiche praied vnto god nothyng el liberally gaue hym vnto hym although greeued hym departe hym erle hauyng bestowed sonne doughter determined lo ger tarry englande well could passed ouer irelande arriued stanford placed hymself seruice man armes beloging erle countrie thinges belong vnto seruing man page knowen cotinued long time great paine toile violenta named gianetta dwelte ladie london grewe yeres beautie personage suche grace fauour lorde ladie rest house well beloued knewe meruailous see men sawe maners countenaunce iudged worthy greate honour possession reason whereof ladie receiued father knowyng reporte purposed marrie honourablie accordyng worthinesse god rewarder mennes desertes knowyng noble woman beare without cause penaunce mannes offence disposed otherwise intente noble gentlewoman might come hades man ill condicion must supposed whiche came passe goddes owne pleasure suffred dooen gentlewoman gianetta dwelt one onely sonne husbande whiche bothe father loued verie dearly well soonne also vertue good merites greatly excelled surpassed good condicions valiaunce goodnesse beautie personage beyng sixe yeres elder gianetta seeyng maiden bee bothe faire comely became farre loue estemed aboue thinges worlde bicause thought base parentage durste demaunde father mother wife fearyng lose fauour kepte loue secrete whereby worse tormented hadde openly knowen thereby chaunced loues malice fill sore sicke whose preseruacion many phisians sente thei markyng hym signes token sickenes knowyng disease altogether doubtfull health whereof father mother tooke greate sorowe grief possible many tymes pitifull praiers thei damaunded hym occasion disease gaue answere nothyng el heauie sighes like consume die weakenesse chaunced vpon daie brought vnto hym phisicion verie younge science profoundlie learned holdyng hym poulces gianetta mother sake attended hym verie carefully entred vpon occasion chamber laie sicke sone yonge gentleman perceiued spake neuer worde made signe demonstracion towardes hym felt harte arise moste amourous defire wherefore poulces beganne beate aboue common custome whiche thyng phisicion immediatly perceiued merualled stadyng still se long fitte would continue gianetta soner gone chamber beatyng poulces ceased wherfore phisicion thought founde parte gentlemannes disease litle seming take occasio speake gianetta holdyng hym still armes caused called incontinently came soner come poulces beganne beate againe departed beatyng ceased whervpon phisicion throughly perswaded vnderstode effecte sicknes therewithall rose vp takyng father mother aside saied vnto health sonne doeth consist helpe phisicions remaineth handes gianetta maide haue perceiued moste manifest signes yonge man feruently dooeth loue yet farre perceiue maiden doeth knowe therefore vnderstande doe loue life gentleman wife hearyng somewhat satisfied muche remedie mighte bee founde saue life athough greued greatly thing wherof thei doubted come passe marriage betwene gianetta soonne phisicion departed thei repaired sicke soonne mother saiyng vnto hym wise soonne would neuer haue thought thou wouldest haue kept secrete parte thy desire specially seyng without thou dooest remaine dauger death thou art ought bee assured nothyng maie gotten thy contetacion euer haue prouided thee ample maner self sith thou haste thus doen chauceth lorde god hath shewed mercie vpon thee thou hasle doen vpo thy self thende thou shalt die disease hath declared vnto cause whiche none great loue thou bearest yonge maide wherso euer bee deede thou oughtest bee ashamed manifest thy loue bicause meete requisite thyne age wist thou couldest loue would lesse esteme thee good sonne afraied franckly discouer thyne affectio driue awaie furie thought whiche thou hast taken whereof sickenes commeth comfort thy self beyng assured thou shalt desire nothyng handes maie doen thy contentacion shall bee accomplished loueth thee better myne owne life therefore expell thee shame feare spare tell able dooe thyng whiche thou louest thou perceiue bee carefull bryng passe repute cruellest mother euer bare childe yonge gentleman hearyng wordes mother first ashamed thinkyng hymself none well able pleasure hym driuyng awaie shame saied wise madame none thyng hath made kepe loue secrete whiche see many people thei bee growen yeres discrecion dooe neuer remember thei haue yonge muche herein dooe see ladiship discrete wise onely affirme true whiche haue perceiued also cofesse vpon suche condicion effect thereof shall folowe promise farre lieth whereby shalbee able recouer life wherevnto mother trusting muche whiche ought haue accomplished certaine consideracions whiche afterwardes came minde answered hym liberally might boldly discouer desire forthwith would bryng passe madame saied yong man greate beautie commendable quality maiden gianetta yet onely haue power intreate take pitie vpon also haue made wight worlde priuie loue disclosyng secrecie wherof hath brought case see thing whiche haue promised dooe one meane come passe assure self life short ladie knowing tyme comforte reprehende saied vnto hym smilyng ala soonne sicke bee good chere whole let alone yong gentleman put good hope shewed litle tyme token signes greate amendemet wherof mother meruellous glad disposyng self proue might obserue whiche promised one daie callyng gianetta vnto demaunded gentle wise waie merie talke gotten louer gianetta face blushyng answered madame haue nede thereof muche vnsemely poore damosell meditate thincke vpon louers whiche banished frendes kinsfolke remainyng seruice dooe ladie saied haue none bestowe one vpo whiche shall content mynde make life delectable pleasaunt nul mete faire maide bee continue without louer wherevnto gianetta answered madame waiyng self haue taken poore father brought vp doughter becometh pleaseth notwithstandyng intende neuer make complainte lacke suche one bothe vertue honestie sake please giue husbande purpose loue hym none progenitours haue left none inheritaunce honestie whiche meane keepe long life indureth woordes ladie semed contrary whiche desired knowe atchieue promes made soonne although like wise ladie self greatly praised damoset said vnto gianetta lorde kyng whiche yonge prince faire maiden would take pleasure loue would refuse hym wherevnto maide sodainly answered kyng maie well force consent shall neuer obtaine thyng except honest ladie conceiuyng courage stoutnesse maiden good parte saied vnto thinkyng put matter proofe tolde sonne whole would put bothe chamber mighte haue pleasure vpon thought dishonest intreate maide sone bicause office roffiana yong man nothing contented therewith whereby sodainly waxed worsse worsse whiche ladie perceiuyng opened whole intente gianetta findyng constaunt euer tolde husbande dooen agreed although willes giue bee wife thinking better sonne liuyng haue wife vnagreable estate suffer hym die sake whiche greate consultacio thei concluded gianetta merueilously well pleased deuoute harte gaue thankes god forgotte yet would neuer name self otherwise doughter picarde yonge sonne waxed whole inco tinently maried best contented man liue began dispose louingly leade life perotto whiche remain wale marshall kyng englade semblably increased welbeloued maister verie comely valiaunt personage like hym founde islande suche wise torneis iustes factes armes none countrie comparable vnto wherfore name perotto picarde knowen renowmed like god forgotten sister euen shewed mercifull remembraunce hym certaine plague mortalitie happened countrie whiche consumed one haulfe people besides moste part liued fledde feare coutries whereby whole prouince seemed bee abandoned desolate whiche plague marshall maister wife sonne many brother neuewes kinsfolke died remained onely doughter mariageable seruauntes together perotto plague somewhat ceased yong gentlewoman toke husbande counsaile consente certaine countrie people aliue bicause valiaunt honest personage inheritaunce whiche father left made hym lorde alitle kyng englande vnderstoode marshall dedde knowyng valor stoutnesse perotto picarde made hym marshall steede dedde sort short tyme chaunced twoo innocent childre erle angiers left hym lost quite forlorne xviij yere sithens erle fledde paris hauyng miserable sorte suffred many aduentures seyng hymself begin ware olde desirous yet ireland knowe could become childre wherefore perceiuyng wholy altred fro wanted forme feelyng hymself lustie long excercise labour whiche susteined seruice idle tyme youthe departed maister verie poore ill apparell continued seruice longe tyme came englande place left perotto founde marshall countrie sawe healthe lustie comely personage whiche reioysed hym merueilously would make hymself knowen hym till seen become doughter gianetta wherefore takyng iourney rested place till came london secretly inquiryng ladie left doughter state learned doughter soonnes wife whereof tooke excedyng greate pleasure tyme forthe compted aduersities past nothing sith founde child liuyng suche greate honor desirous see began like poore manne harbour hymself harde house wherevpon certain daie beyng seen giachetto lamyens name husbade gianetta hauing pitie vpo bicause sawe hym poore olde commaunded one seruauntes haue hym house giue hym meate goddes sake whiche seruaunt willingly accomplish gianetta many child giachetto whiche eldest eight yeres olde thei fairest beste fauoured child worlde thei sawe erle eate meate thei came aboute hym began make muche hym thoughe nature instruction thei knowen grandfather knowyng nephewes began shewe token loue kindnesse reason whereof child would goe hym although gouernour call awaie wherefore mother knowing came chamber vnto place erle threatened beare thei would doe maister hadde child began crie saied thei would tary good manne loued better maister whereat ladie erle began laugh erle father like poore man rose vp dooe honour doughter bicause noble woman conceiuyng merueilous ioye minde see knewe hym neither instant bicause wonderfully transformed chaunged forme wonte bee like one olde graie hedded hauyng bearde leane weather beaten resemblyng rather common persone erle ladie seyng child would departe still cried thei fetched awaie willed maister lette alone child remainyng sorte honest poore manne father giacchetto came meane time vnderstoode maister wherefore cared gianetta saied lette alone mischief keepe companie beggers thei came mother side thei bee verlettes child therefore meruaile though thei loue companie erle hearing wordes verie sorowfull notwithstadyng holdyng doune hedde suffred iniurie well hadde doen many giacchetto knewe mirth ioye child made poore man although offended woordes neuerthelesse made muche poore erle sawe wepe commaunded honest poore man would dwell doe seruice bee reteined answered would carie good said could doe nothyng el kepe horsse wherevnto accustomed day life horsse appoincted keepe daily whe dressed horsse gaue hymself plaie child while fortune thus dealt accordyng maner aboue saied erle angiers child chaunced frenche kyng many truce made almaignes gouernemente perotto marshall giacchetto lamyens soonne marshall poore erle wente knowen man remained greate campe seruaunt notwithstandyng like valiaunt man aduise deedes accomplished notable thinges onely deede also thought abandoned companie men excepte thy husbande wherof shalbe right pensife sorowfull long litle remnaunte life myne olde age doeth preserue indureth sith thou couldest conteine cruell vnto thee notwithstandyng dooe make certaine resolucion desire heare thou canst saie thy self spoken wordes kissed face wepyng verie bitterly like child beaten gismonda hearyng father knowyng guiscardo ought deare father knowe self fleshe fleshe haue engendred doughter stone iron likewise ought muste remember although arriued olde yeres yonge folkes great power law youth although duryng force youthlie day trained exercised factes armes yet ought knowe greate puissaunce resteth idle delicate life aswell aged emonges yonge people bee begotten fleshe yeres fewe yet yonge thereby full luste delight wherevnto knowledge haue alredie mariage forceth accoplishe desire added merueilous force againste whiche impossible resist rather followe wherevnto thei draw become amourous like yong woma like woma certainly would haue imploied whole force waie farre could commit shame self wherevnto naturall offence hath forced whiche thyng pitifull loue gentle fortune haue founde shewed waie secrete enough whereby without knowledge man come effect desire whiche thyng deny euer tolde meanes euer come knowledge therof haue taken guiscardo louer chaunce many wome haue doen haue chosen hym long aduise deliberacion aboue others haue brought wise inioiyng wise continuaunce long time accomplishment desire wherof thinke although haue offended loue doe purpose prosecute rather vulgar opinio truthe purposyng wise bitterly coptroll saiyng suche occasion anger chosen one gentleman wherein doe consider fault mine rather ascribed fortune ought bee blamed bicause many tymes exalteth vnworthie treadeth vnder foote moste worthie let v leaue talke matter consider beginnyng hereof firste see one masse fleshe wee haue receiued fleshe one creatour hath created euery liuing creature force puissance equally equall vertue whiche vertue first occasion made difference distinccion v borne bee borne equall thei obteined greatest parte vertue workes called noble rest continuyng vnnoble albeit man ought praised haue doen truely without cause mine eye deceiued neuer gaue hym praise haue knowen hym woordes able expresse notwithstandyng haue deceiued herein haue deceiued saie couple self manne base condicion truelie well saie saie perchaunce poore man confesse verely shame haue vouchesaufed place high estate manne honest beyng owne seruaunt neuerthelesse pouertie doeth depriue part nobilitie rich hath many kinges greate prince haue poore olde tyme many plough men shepherdes time paste haue aduauced riche estate last doubte whiche troubleth bee doubtfull dooe caste boldlie mynde doubte doe intende thextremitie age vse whiche youth neuer purpose become cruel also use crueltie aduoidyng wherof haue determined make supplicacion giltie fault faultes maie bee rehearsed assuryng dooe vnto whiche haue dooen dooe guiscardo myne owne handes shall dooe wherefore goe let fall teares woman purpose cruell kill lette also drincke cuppe thinke wee haue deserued kyng hearyng stoute wordes doughter thought would haue doen deede wordes pretended saied would dooe wherefore departyng willyng vse maner crueltie towardes thought destruction slaughter guiscardo coole burnyng loue therefore commaunded twoo seruauntes guiscardo kepyng without noise strangle hym next night afterwardes pluckyng harte bodie bryng vnto thei commaunded nexte daie kyng caused faier cuppe golde bee brought vnto hym wherein laied harte guiscardo whiche sente one familer seruauntes vnto doughter commaunded hym presented vnto saie woordes thy father hath sent thee present comforte thy self thyng whiche thou doest chieflie loue thou hast comforted hym whiche loued moste gismonda amoued fro cruell determinacio caused brought vnto father gone venemous herbes rootes whiche distilled together made water thereof drincke sodainly came passe whiche doubted kynges seruaunt come vnto deliuered presente saied commaunded gismonda tooke cuppe stoute countenaunce coueryng sone sawe harte vnderstoode wordes thought verely harte guiscardo wherefore beholdyng seruaunt said vnto truely behoueth suche harte bee intombed worsse graue gold whiche father hath moste wisely doen afterwardes liftyng cuppe mouthe kissed saiyng haue thynges euen vnto time last ende life alwaies founde tender loue father towardes knowe bee greater euer therefore behalfe shall render vnto hym last thankes euer shall giue hym greate presente woordes tourning self towardes cuppe whiche helde fast beholdyng harte saied thus oh sweete harborough pleasure cursed crueltie hym hath caused tyme looke vpon thee eye face pleasure enoughe see thee euery hower emonges people knowledge vnderstanding thou hast finished thy course ende whiche fortune vouchsaufed giue thee thou art dispatched arriued ende wherevnto men haue recourse thou hast forsaked misery traueiles worlde hast enemie hymself suche sepulture thy worthinesse deserueth needeth nothyng el accomplishe thy funeralle onely teares thou diddest hartely loue al day thy life hauing whereof lorde putte heade vnmercifull father sende thee vnto truely bestowe teares vpon thee although determined die without sheadyng teares stoutlie fearfull thyng haue powred thee cause soule whiche thou hast heretofore carefully kept ioyned thine companie trauell contented better saufgarde place vnknowen thy soule truely well assured yet within hath respecte place aswell owne pleasure myne beyng assured certaine yet loueth attenddeth soule greatly beloued thus saied began let fall though fountaine hedde many teares miracle beholde ofte tymes kissyng dedde harte maiden stode aboute vnderstoode harte wherevnto wordes tende beyng moued compassion thei wept pitifullie demaunding although vaine occasion sorowfull plaintes comforted well thei could powred sufficient teares lifted vp hedde wiped hereyes saied oh louyng harte duetie fulfilled towardes thee hauyng nothyng doe onely yelde forthe ghoste accopanie thine saied caused glasse water whiche made daie bee bewitched onely consumed day nightes burned continual ialousie whose beautie liuely painted inwarde partes harte mynde remained thus ouerwhelmed beastly pleasure euery man particuler generall conspired hym one determinate minde yelde obedience vnto hym tyme come purposed chose emperour marciall warlike whose succour counsaile thei might onely conserue thynges gotten also amplifie boundes limites empire mustapha whiche broughte vp emperour gentle personage franke talke nere maiestie might goe chamber although greke present perceiued conueniente tyme suche desired haue repaired emperour vpon daie likyng wel deuises walked hym alone gardein made greate reuerence accordyng custome saied vnto hym soueraigne lorde maister might speake freelie without seruile feare whiche staieth terrour maie bee eye bounde vp vaile disordinate affection digest take good part life lorde whiche haue ledde sithens taking constantinople excessiue pleasure wherein haue pludged self three yeres occasion occasion chaste ladie rapt wittes straungenes case grief whiche conceiued see vnshamefast hardinesse varlette could tell make hym answere ende breakyng silence fetchyng great sighe bottome hec harte face slained fresh uermilion rudde whiche beautified colour reason disdaine conceiued impudent orator answered hym verie seuerely god would haue thought hart nobly brought vp deriued honourable race villanie greate could haue taken roote spryng vp suche detestable fruicte maister stewarde haue ye forgotten duetie seruaunt towarde lorde maister haue ye forgotten saie duetie vertuous gentleman well nourished trained vp towarde suche greate ladie ah traitour thou art venime whiche thou kepest couert secrete vnder swetenesse thy counterfaicte vertue vaunte varlette vaunte goe vtter thy stuffe like thy self whose honour honeslie farre spent thy loialtie lighte vaine heare thee speake folly bee assured mortifie ragyng flame whiche burneth thy light beleuyng harte make thee feele effecte maner death wherein thou reposeste rest thy trauell deceued oratour framyng excuse aboute moderate iuste wrathe ladie displeased vpon good occasion able abide talke saied signes dishonestie haste thou seen moue thee perswade thing wicked vncomely myne estate yea preiudiciall frendes house thy maister lorde spouse tell letteth causyng thee bee caste emong lion cruell capitall enemy adulterie emonges selfes sithe thy pretence violatyng chastite dishonor house wherevnto thou owest lesse aduauncemente thou haste taste whereof thou haste abandoned uertue best thyng wherewith thou affected auoide therefore let heare vpon paine thy life otherwise thou shalt feele rewarde thy teinerite vnderstande bitternesse litle pleasure whiche haue conceiued thy folly good ladie helde peace reseruyng harte whiche helpe tyme place howbeit said nothyng hereof vnto husbande aswell raisyng offence slaunder prouokyng husbande whiche susteined punishement sithe refuse straungely pinche hym nere harte euer egle caucasus whereof poetes haue talked muche tier mawe subtil prometheus yet vnhappie steward contentented mischief co mitted honor maister seing yt lost time cotinue pursute gaine would bee lesse muche hym owne persone side knewe longe ladie aliue could haue maner ioye contentacion cause conuerting extreme loue whiche bare ladie cruell hatred vnsemelie brutall beast insaciable desire reuenge determined addresse strong ambushe trained suche subteltie able escape without daunger life honor whereof declared self carefull ala blindnes whiche captiuateth wittes spirite hym feedeth hymself nothyng el vpon rage fantasticall despite vpon furie despaire doe se reason giueth place desired reuenge wronge thought receiued man dispoyleth hymself whiche apperteineth kinde man put fierce nature moste brute cruell beastes runne hedlong without reason toward place disordinate appetite affection doeth conducte hym whereof aduouche example traitour passionated loue rather rage furie ceaseth espie al action behauiour ladie intente might bryng ende deuised treason thought perchaunce folie honestlie passe tyme deare wel beloued husbande truely ladie disposicion woman care moleste husbandes firste flie buzzeth eye conceiuyng friuelous sodaine opinio chastitie muche asiailed sharpelie defended chauntyng glorious hympnes high praise victorie certainlie tombled self daunger wherevnto afterwardes fill blame doe reueale husbandes assaultes whiche thei receiue importunate suters doe assaie deflower chastite yet saie mosdestie euery humaine actio greatly required sith suche one thinkyng extolle honour honestie make proofe chastite rendreth suspicious giueth occasion talke people apt redie slaunder infamie good reporte praise whiche vertue doe deserue comme dacion bringyng life fame husbande suche extremitie better vertuouslie haue resisted force loue flatteryng sute suche louers manifest whiche mighte haue kept secrete without preiudice either partes truely woman deserueth greater glorie self defendeth honestie quencheth flame liuely kindled harte coldnesse continencie meanes vanquishing twoo doeth whiche manifesting vice discloseth certain apparaunce frailtie requeste indewed reason abandon pleasure reiecte insolencie sithe reason force doeth easely vanquishe lighte affeccions sensuall partie one ingrauen fantasie doe make sens woman inconstant thei perswade themselfes bee puissaunt mightie thinges rest pleasure retournyng former discourse stewarde laboured might maine till founde meanes bee reuenged receiued refusall suche subtiltie deuelishe inuencion possible manne deuise whiche emong seruauntes greate lorde one lesse yonge witte vnderstandyng age albeit faier comelie yet simple foolishe muche doe tell nomber sixe foole reason folly simplicitie onely sporte passetyme lorde ladie ladie many tymes tooke pleasure talke maister foole bring hym choler chaufe thereby prouoke laughter therefore housholde vsed call hym mockerie lady darelyng lorde tooke singuler pleasure delight estemyng hym well seruauntes malicious steward seyng familiaritie ladie fole like one alredie catched praie within snare began also make muche yonge cockescome suche wise broughte hym suche fooles paradise might make hym doe saie list seyng hym diligent desire one daie tooke hym side hadde whittled hym well saied vnto dicke tel thee knacke thou shalt make ladie laugh well thou muste saie nothyng till dooe perceiue poore idiot glad please maistres desirous knowe promised dooe euer would bidde hym thou said stewarde euenyng goe chamber hide thy self vnder bedde tary till bee hower twoo daie tell thee thou must doe platte deuised foole euenyng executed deuise deuelishe counsailour seyng desire take effecte went olde gentleman greate stroken flashe lightenyng drawing nere accuser answered possible suche wickednesse canne lie hidden breast madame sweare vnto thee god tolde besides would haue beleued truely yet doubt thereof saied afflicted minde without comfort consolacion creature liuyng dure cruell penaunce doe susteine none offence ah fortune fortune enemie felicite blisse thou haste depriued remedie dare muche make manne knowe vnderstande mishappe might reuenged whiche beyng dooen would render suche contentacion mynde departe worlde best contented satisfied maiden euer died ala goddes graunte benefite might haue come noble kinde thintent might haue caused traiterous ruffien feele grieuous paine bitter tormentes whiche poore harte susteineth ah wretched caitife abadoned forlorne good fortune doe see eye mynde whiche bodie daseled deceiued could see perceiue ah cruell enemie pitie doest thou knowe feele thy minde heauie sorowful sounde bitter plaintes understandest thou voice crieth vengeaunce vpon thee thy misdeede thy crueltie nothyng diminished seyng dismembred terrour thousande furious martirdomes ah ingrate wretche rewarde loue faithfull seruice myne obediece thus bitterly tormented self mother brother maide whiche brought vp teder yeres went vp chamber violenta thei foude deformed rage furie almost knowledge thei went reduce meanes possible furious panges saw nothing auailed thei left keping old maiden loued aboue maiden vttered vnto particularly many reason appeasyng grief tolde would quiet little would goe speake knight didaco make hym vnderstande fault would discret order deale come home house therfore praied arme self againste wickednes dissemble matter time hereafter might vse vpon hym iust reuenge ianique answered violenta offece small light counsaill receiued albeit ca chose confesse thy counsaill meete yet wanteth mynde followe feele parte disposed obeye would euen thy face separate mynde fro wretched bodie resolued malice hatred didaco satisfie without life alone beleue goddes cause borne myne owne handes execute vengeaunce wrathe losse myne honour wherefore ianique fro youth thou diddest euer loue shewe effect matter whervnto thy helpe moste necessary outraged mischief doe enuie ye miserablest creature worlde remainyng continue life wailyng continuall sighes title vile abhominable whore thou art straunger liuest beastly life ioyned continuall deceiued albeeit thesame bee doen secretly ende must knowen yet doubt cause declared iudges thei vnderstandyng wronge hath doen thei haue compassion vpon miserie knowe right well alwaies haue knowen sorowe vnder painfull silence thinkyng olde promisses confirmed many othes assured proofe still haue faithe constauncie would haue broughte order seyng myne eye hard mettall harte crueltie fate whiche wholie hath subdued obedience respecte myne honour forced complaine hym beateth thereby dispoileth bothe myne honor life vouchsaufyng onely muche one come vnto vncertaine maie make recourse fined redress appeale vnto thende seyng leane vglie state crueltie maie altogether satisfied whiche beholdyng sight pitifull wherein figure torment liuelie expressed maie moued compassion come hither thou cruell man come hither saie visite signe humanite thou maiest staie least wise mollifie appease vengeaunce whiche prepareth thee euer spark pitie warme thy frosen harte arme thy self greater crueltie euer thou wont come hither make sobbe laste extreme sighes thou hast wretchedly deceiued doyng otherwise thou maiest peraduenture late bewaile death thy beastly crueltie thinking make conclusion letter teares made wordes die mouthe would suffer write wherefore closed sealed thesame callyng ianique vnto saied holde gentle ianique cary letter vnto hym thou canst well plaie thy part haue doen myne hope shall haue shortly commaundemente hym occasion painfull life greuous vnto thousande deathes together ianique hauyng letter departed diligence went house father lawe didaco quietly waited
